Abyssinian Army's Morale Greatly Boosted 46

Akyab: According to a dispatch from our correspondent, O'Chana, fierce battles have continued on the northern front line in recent days, but there has been no change in the lines of either side. The Abyssinian army won the fierce battle in the Tembien region. Although the positions have not moved and Magdala, Axum, and Adowa are still occupied by the Italian army, the morale of the Abyssinian army has been greatly boosted. They believe that the victory in this battle can be compared to the Battle of Adowa forty years ago. In addition, with the rainy season approaching, the Italian army is not accustomed to this kind of weather, and the war will inevitably be suspended. Therefore, the Abyssinian side is more and more satisfied. As for the southern front line, although it is still quiet on the surface, the government is quite concerned. According to palace sources, the Italian army has crossed 320 kilometers beyond Dolo in three days and has built a strong line of fortifications in the Neghelli area, which is a good base for mechanized units to set out for reconnaissance. At this moment, the Italian army is trying to completely clear the area between Neghelli and British Kenya, and to cut off the roads around Moyale (on the Kenyan border), so that the Abyssinian army will not be able to receive military supplies from that area. (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Change of Commander on the Southern Abyssinian Front 47

Akyab: After General Dejazmatch Desta Damtew, the commander of the southern front, was defeated by Italian General Graziani, the Emperor has ordered the veteran General Balcha Safo, a member of the Imperial Council, to command the armies on the southern front and recover the lost territories. Balcha is old in age and once commanded artillery under the former Emperor Menelik, with outstanding achievements in the Battle of Adowa in 1896. He is known for his strong will, extraordinary bravery, and is highly revered by his soldiers. In addition, the Minister of Interior, Gebre Mariam, will soon go to Sidamo province on the southern front for inspection, while the Minister of Finance, Fekre Selassie, will go to Bale to take over the command of General Mulugeta's troops, and Mulugeta will replace Desta's troops. Mulugeta once stopped the Italian army from advancing at the Webi Shebelle River and is also one of Abyssinia's famous generals. According to Abyssinian military observers, the patriotic spirit of the Abyssinian army is higher than ever before, and the Italian army's right wing in the south will soon feel threatened. General Nasibu Emmanual, the commander of the Ogaden province in the east, also seems to be preparing to switch to offensive tactics. (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Scientific Talks: On Afforestation for Air Defense (Part 2) 48

— Edited by the Science Society of China, Li Yin-kung

Europeans and Americans are accustomed to respecting international law and the agreements between friendly countries, and they are willing to abide by the so-called diplomatic creeds. When it comes to military aviation equipment, flight takeoffs and landings usually have rules and must not cross the line. This is to avoid misunderstandings and discourtesy. Our country's northern region is often invaded and patrolled by foreign air forces for military exercises. Protests have been heard many times, but those who rely on their strength and act recklessly ignore them. Their ulterior motives can be imagined. Therefore, for those who seek self-defense, for the sake of preparing for a rainy day, they have to urgently plant trees for defense. The author occasionally checked a newspaper on his desk, which contained an aerial photograph of a part of the city of Meudon, France, showing other countries the lush cityscape of trees.

Most of the cities in our country's provinces have few trees, let alone small towns. When I lived in Anqing in the past, I had to rely on written publicity every winter and spring. One title was "Anqing, where birds cannot land." The language was satirical, so as to promote people's awareness. In the past, Kang Youwei traveled to Kaifeng and published his poems on the Iron Pagoda, "Looking into the distance, the high and cold overlooks Bianzhou, the Iron Pagoda of Fantai floats with the clouds. Ten thousand families have no trees and no palaces, but see the Yellow River rolling." His intention to express his feelings can also be seen. Now, at a time when foreign troubles are frequent, afforestation for air defense in areas near cities and towns seems to be something that cannot be ignored. From December to February, it is the best time of year for afforestation. All native tree species (fast-growing ones are excellent) can be used to decorate the scenery.

Now we may as well think of the suburbs. On the country roads in late autumn and frost, woodcutters probably account for more than half of the pedestrians. Carts are pulled and shoulders are burdened, all of which are mountain grass and wild saplings, mixed together and sold in the city as firewood. Among them, there are many miscellaneous trees with a diameter of one inch to two inches. If they are allowed to be preserved for three to five years, it will not be difficult to form a forest. Villagers cut down trees to burn charcoal, and they will not hesitate to cut down trees with a diameter of five to seven inches. Alas. If our country does not have a forestry policy for a day, when will this trend stop? If you talk to the woodcutters about afforestation for air defense, they will definitely think that you are talking to the wrong person. Who knows that all wild trees are the basis of the natural forests of the heavy forest country, which is the easiest way to cultivate them, and there is no need to worry about diseases, pests, and floods. Try taking a survey of the percentage of wild trees protected in the Wulong Mountain area of the capital:

Ratio 92955055555555 out of 100647601000000 hundred and one wild tree name Quercus aliena var. acuteserrata, Betula platyphylla, Lindera obtusiloba, Sophora japonica, Sapium sebiferum, Liquidambar formosana, Ulmus parvifolia, Diospyros kaki, Ailanthus altissima, Celtis sinensis, Acer buergerianum

The above table shows the composition of natural tree species near the capital. If afforestation for air defense is carried out in the capital, it can be used as a basic tree species. Other places may also take it as an example. Here, I would like to solemnly suggest: If you want to engage in air defense, you must plant trees. In urban areas, if each household plants five to ten trees, this goal can be achieved. In my humble opinion, this is the simplest and most economical way to save oneself and the country. A great disaster is inevitable in the future. If this is done to reduce the panic, then this is the author's humble wish.

Egypt Prepares to Begin Treaty Negotiations with Britain 70

London: Preparations are underway in Cairo to reopen negotiations between Egyptian representatives and British Officer Lampson, in order to produce a draft alliance and resolve the four items reserved when Britain relinquished Egypt as its protectorate in 1922. These four items are: 1. British Empire's communication routes, including the Suez Canal. 2. Egypt's defense against external aggression. 3. Protection of foreign interests, including minorities. 4. The status of Sudan. Since Maher formed a neutral new government in Egypt, the tension between Britain and Egypt has eased. All parties in Egypt have now formed a delegation of the same front, and newspapers believe that the negotiations are bound to succeed. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

French Dockworkers Threaten a General Strike 71

Saint-Nazaire: A dispute broke out between labor and management at a large shipyard here yesterday. The dockworkers decided to strike, and it is feared that a general strike of French dockworkers will erupt as a result. The workers have been dissatisfied with wages and working conditions for a long time. They were angered by a notice posted by the employer yesterday, believing that this notice was very different from the remarks made by the joint labor-management committee. The workers' leader instructed the workers to stop work, and the crowd followed. Although it is still quiet at the moment, the labor unrest may spread on Sunday, because the strikers are now planning to send pickets to other shipyards to prevent work. It is expected that if a general strike is realized, the launch ceremony of the new French cruiser Georges Leygues, scheduled for February 24, will be postponed, and the construction of the 35,000-ton cruiser Strasbourg will also be delayed. Today, the joint labor-management committee specially convened a meeting to reconcile the dispute between the two parties, but the vote of the factory representatives unanimously approved the strike immediately. One of the factory representatives has now been sent to Le Havre to induce the workers working on the large merchant ship Normandie to stop work altogether. (Reuters dispatch, 2nd)

The Famous Play "Peony Pavilion" Gains Good Reviews in Vienna 73

Vienna: Professor Hong Tao-sheng, a German who has lived in China for many years, has translated famous Chinese legends such as "Peony Pavilion" and "Romance of the West Chamber" into scripts and organized a troupe. He left Peking last summer to perform in Germany. Recently, he came to Austria from Germany and performed "Peony Pavilion" for the first time yesterday at the Hofburg Theater here. This is the first time that Chinese drama has been performed in Austria. The play "Peony Pavilion" was originally a famous legend of the 16th century. Yesterday, the protagonist Du Liniang was played by Ms. Younge Lucy. Ms. Younge's father is German, and her mother is Chinese. She has performed old Chinese dramas in Peking, Tianjin, and other places and has received extremely good reviews. This time, she came to Europe with a Chinese orchestra to play music for the play. There is no set on the stage, only a long black curtain is used as a background, and the actors perform in front of the curtain. Although there is no set, the sincerity of the performance is amazing. The entire play is translated into German poetry. The actors recite the lines and perform the movements at the same time. Although the movements have a fixed routine, they are not cumbersome and are very subtle. Only the facial expressions are not full. The first performance of the play was "Chunxiang's Study," followed by "A Dream in the Garden." Ms. Younge's performance, in the midst of singing and dancing, made the audience hold their breath and listen. This is very different from Western opera, which emphasizes loud singing and fast dancing. Although the Austrian people may not be able to understand it immediately, the intellectual class in Vienna has praised it endlessly. If the troupe continues to gain good reviews in other capitals in Europe, the Western stage will inevitably be gradually influenced by Chinese drama in the future and adopt its strengths, because the plot of Chinese drama is simple and can best lead people to return to the common psychology of mankind. (Havas dispatch, 2nd)

Japanese Model Village Becomes Scorched Earth 74

Yokohama: Jojima, Miura District, Kanagawa Prefecture, known as a peaceful and beautiful place, suddenly experienced a fire at 2:10 AM on the 2nd. At that time, due to the southwest wind, the fire was extremely fierce and could not be extinguished. More than 120 households, including famous temples and other private houses, were completely burned down, resulting in the complete destruction of the island. The fire gradually subsided at 6:00 AM. The island has been free of fire for 150 years, and none of the residents have committed any crimes. It can be called a peaceful and model village. Now, it has suddenly turned into scorched earth, which makes people sigh. (Allied News Agency dispatch, 2nd)

Anxi Mining Work: Chen Ticheng Reports That Ore May Be Sold to Japan 75

Japanese Technician Talks About Hoping for Joint Chinese-Japanese Investment in Amoy Communication: The Anxi Mining Exploration Team organized by the Construction Department of the Fujian Provincial Government, led by Zhao Xiujin, the director of the Anxi Iron Mine Exploration Project Office, and thirteen Japanese technicians from the South Manchuria Railway Company, set off from Amoy on January 3rd and arrived in Anxi County on the 4th. They gathered in Hukou on the 12th. The Japanese consulate in Amoy also sent consulate officials Ikeda and Fan Zhongchang to accompany them. However, after arriving in Hukou, they were unable to go to their destination, Pantian, due to the unrest caused by bandits in the mountains. The two consulate officials, Ikeda and Fan, returned to Amoy on the 14th. Later, with the protection of the Sixth Security Regiment, the mining exploration team arrived in Pantian in late January and started working separately. After the mining exploration team entered Anxi, local schools and organizations, not knowing the details, rose up to oppose them. Later, after the county government and the Sixth Regiment explained that this was an exploration and the Japanese technicians were actually hired, the public opinion gradually subsided. As for the deputy director Lin Chao-chin, he led four Japanese technicians and set off from Amoy by water on January 3rd, traveling up the Jiulong River to Hua'an Zhangping, surveying the water conservancy and harbors along the way, and returning to Amoy on the 12th. The Japanese technicians Igarashi and Soma returned to Taiwan. This mining exploration work is divided into four parts: 1. Surveying the estuary, harbors, and waterways for transportation. 2. Investigating the railway line and land transportation from Anxi to the estuary. 3. Exploring the mine. 4. Test drilling. Each part is equipped with Japanese technicians from the South Manchuria Railway. 1. The survey of harbors and waterways has been completed. 2. The survey of the railway line. 3. Mine exploration. These two items can be completed in two or three months. 4. Test drilling. This will take ten months. It is necessary to use a diamond drill bit to drill three holes 200 meters deep to measure the amount of mineral reserves. The work is very complicated. Regarding the Anxi mining exploration, Chen Ticheng, the Director of the Construction Department, recently reported at a memorial weekly meeting of the provincial government, roughly saying, "The Anxi iron mine was surveyed in the first step last March and April. As a result, it was recognized that the mineral quality is very good, with iron accounting for 66% to 67%, manganese accounting for 3%, and sulfur and phosphorus accounting for 0.05%. The rest are impurities. Among the iron mines that have been mined in our country, the mineral quality in Hubei and Anhui provinces is the best, but iron only accounts for 50%. Therefore, the mineral reserves in Anxi are the most abundant. According to the report of the Geological Survey Institute of our country, there are 10 million tons of reserves in Pantian alone, and Japanese experts estimate that the total amount reaches 48 million tons. To this end, the second step of drilling is carried out. Drilling machines are extremely expensive and difficult to purchase on our own. Therefore, we borrowed them from the Japanese side and hired several Japanese technicians to work in four parts. The harbor and railway parts are needed for land and water transportation after mining, so they are also involved. If the investigation results show that it is worth mining, a decision can be made. There are two main outlets for mineral production: 1. Establishing our own iron smelting plant. 2. Selling the ore. Judging from the situation in our province, iron smelting requires coal and limestone, but the output in our province is very small. Bai coal in Longyan is not suitable, and although there is bituminous coal in northern Fujian, transportation is not easy. When selling broken ore, where should the market be, will also be considered. The iron ore in Hubei and Anhui is mostly sold to Japan. If the Anxi mine is mined, in addition to promoting the ore to various parts of our country, it may also need to be sold to Japan." After the Japanese technicians Igarashi and Soma returned to Taiwan, Igarashi gave a speech saying, "Mr. Soma, Yoshida, and I have worked together in the South Manchuria Railway Company for many years. This time, we are sincerely invited by the Fujian Provincial Government to have the opportunity to practice the iron mountain range in southern Fujian. The mineral area that our team inspected in Hua'an Zhangping is very easy to establish a transportation route linking Xiamen and the central terminal. The ore output is definitely a natural wealth with endless reserves, and there is no technical problem. We also hope that the two friendly countries, China and Japan, will be further friendly and invest together in development." (February 1st)

Special Relief Products of Fujian Province: Last Year, Fuzhou's Imports Exceeded Exports by More Than 3 Million; Provincial Government Plans to Formulate Measures for Relieving Special Products 76

Fuzhou Correspondence: The three products of tea, timber, and paper in Fujian Province are indeed the province's major special products. In the past, tea and timber exports from Fuzhou alone were valued at over 10 million yuan annually. Now, they are only worth three to four million yuan. Paper exports from Fuzhou were valued at over four million yuan annually; now, they are only worth over 800,000 yuan. Consequently, many trading houses in Fuzhou dealing in these products have closed down, and many farmers and workers in the upper reaches of the Min River who plant and manufacture these products have also lost their jobs. Upon investigation, the reasons are: Firstly, northern Fujian has suffered from banditry for many years, and most farmers have fled, leaving the mountains uncultivated, resulting in a significant reduction in production. Secondly, most of the paper was sold to the three northeastern provinces. Since the fall of those provinces, the puppet state has established customs and imposed high import taxes. Most of the timber was sold to various parts of North China. In recent years, the situation in North China has been unstable, and the market has been declining daily. Most of the tea was sold to various islands in Southeast Asia. Recently, the market has been captured by tea from Ceylon and India. As a result, Fuzhou's foreign trade, which used to be a surplus port, saw imports exceed exports by more than three million yuan last year. Last autumn, the provincial government's statistics office conducted a survey of the province's special products, concluding that if no active measures were taken to relieve these three special products, the province's economic future would have little hope. However, this is a significant matter, and after detailed planning, it has recently been decided that, concerning the relief of the paper industry, the first step will be to reduce taxes. Starting from March 1st of this year, the special business tax on paper products will be reduced by one-third of the original tax rate, and the business tax on paper manufacturing will also be changed to a levy of 0.5%. This has been communicated to the Fuzhou Tax Bureau and the governments of various paper-producing counties in northwestern Fujian for compliance. Regarding the relief of the tea industry, it has been decided to guide tea farmers to improve their production methods. As the new spring tea is about to bud, the local governments of tea-producing counties are immediately ordered to organize rural cooperatives. The provincial government will allocate 300,000 yuan to be lent to the cooperatives for re-lending to farmers as funds for improving tea production. Tokyo Correspondence

Fierce Competition in Japan's "Election Purification" (3) 77

— Hengzhi

——As a Transition for War Preparations in "Extraordinary Times"——

The Social Mass Party advocates for "nationalization of important industries" and prioritizes "domestic reform first." Their central platform is as follows:

(1) Construction of Labor Parliament Politics

(2) Opposition to Mass Tax Increases

(3) Immediate Implementation of a National Pension System

(4) Establishment of Public Industrial and Commercial Financial Institutions

(5) Nationalization of Important Industries

(6) National Compensation for Agricultural Losses

The central slogans of the Social Mass Party are:

(1) Domestic Reform First

(2) National Defense Can Only Be Secure with a Prosperous Populace

(3) The Past? The Future? Already a Political Party? The Mass Party?

They assess the situation in various times and places and appropriately select these slogans. Although they did not win more than ten seats in the initial elections, they have proven that tens of thousands of working masses support them. Of course, in the "extraordinary times" situation, the future of parliamentary competition is also very limited.

(4)

Under the slogan of "national unity" of the current cabinet and the Minseitō (Constitutional Democratic Party), there are naturally many inconsistencies between facts and propaganda. The reverse side of "purifying the election" is the existence of "non-purification." This is a problem that cannot be eliminated in capitalist countries.

Looking at the policies and slogans of the above parties, what is displayed before us is:

(1) The Seiyūkai (Rikken Seiyūkai - Friends of Constitutional Government Party) clearly represents the current will of a part of the financial capitalists: both industrial and national defense. On this point, although the Minseitō even shouts "three aspects of national defense, industry, and finance," from the point of view that the Minseitō is the current cabinet party, this proposition is not as powerful as the Seiyūkai, and also contains some differences in composition. Because since the Manchurian Incident, the Japanese territory, whether economic, political, or military, has already expanded. However, the expansion of the military territory has been faster. In order to cultivate and strengthen the existing foundations on this expanded territory, some parts of financial capital must hope for a longer period of stability. If this longer period of stability does not exist, then not only will the profits of capital not be sufficient, but the burden of increased military spending will not be easily compensated. Since this increased burden cannot be fully borne by the colonies, a part of it has to be placed on the domestic working masses. However, at present, except for the military-related industries, there is no particularly prosperous time. Adding to the burden of the masses will ignite domestic problems. Therefore, even if the alias "extraordinary times" is used for the "major current situation," it is impossible not to sing "national defense and industry together."

(2) On the anti-fascist point, the Social Mass Party shouts out this slogan, and the Minseitō also publicly defines it as one of its political platforms. The Seiyūkai avoids this frontal conflict. However, both the Seiyūkai and the Minseitō advocate parliamentary politics, so they also have some anti-fascist substance and appearance. Since the Manchurian Incident, various kinds of fascist tendencies have gradually become clear; however, a unified fascist party has not yet fully formed. This also means that the fascism of the small bourgeois mass movement incited by a certain faction of financial capital has not fully formed in Japan. However, judging from the anti-fascist slogans shouted by several factions in this election, the fascist forces are also not small; at the same time, we can see its military power.

(3) Judging from the Japanism advocated by the Kokumin Dōmei (National League), and even more from its advocacy of the consistency of military action and diplomatic action, this is clearly aimed at the other parties. However, it does not want to say that it is fascist. However, it undoubtedly advocates strengthening Japan's continental policy. Of course, as it currently appears, the number of people he can be elected to will at most not exceed twenty or thirty people.

(4) What has attracted the attention of all parties is the participation of the Social Mass Party of the proletariat camp in the election. The parliamentary struggles of the Proletarian Party in countries such as Germany have had many successes and failures. In the sense of expressing a certain aspect of the will of the labor group, striving for public propaganda, and allowing it to openly express anti-fascism, it is certainly sufficient to attract the attention of all parties. In fact, the fascist forces, starting from the officials, have already been infiltrated into a part of the working masses. "The construction of labor parliament politics" cannot be produced at present, but it can be shouted like this. "Opposing the increase of mass taxes" may have some effect. "Nationalization of important industries" - this will be used for military control of the national economy, right? In short, this should be seen as their current possible public movement. In one of their slogans, "implement domestic reform first," this is the most different place from other factions.

(5) Although the general election on February 20 has not yet arrived, the decision of the parliament and the cabinet can be roughly inferred from the current election situation. The Kokumin Dōmei, Showakai (Showa Society), Social Mass Party, etc. in the 466 prescribed seats, at most, can occupy sixty or so seats. Because the Kokumin Dōmei and the Showakai are the most supportive of the government - even the Kokumin Dōmei is supportive of the military, the number of seats will have an increasing trend. The current Seiyūkai and Minseitō are competing for the first party. In the initial election, the Minseitō had twenty or thirty fewer seats than the Seiyūkai, and because of the current cabinet's assistance, it is working hard to surpass the Seiyūkai, and in fact, it is indeed somewhat possible to surpass it. However, the situation has been slightly determined, and the seats of these two major parties will not be very different. These two major parties were born from the same mother (Japanese capitalism), and it doesn't matter much who is in power. However, if the Minseitō gets a majority of seats, it will be more glorious for the current cabinet's face. But if you don't listen to the military's command of more than 50%, you can't do it, so the so-called anti-fascism is equal to being anti-yourself. If the Seiyūkai occupies a majority, the cabinet will naturally collapse without face, but the reform marked out by the Seiyūkai is not fundamentally different from the current cabinet. Moreover, if you don't coordinate with the military, even if the Seiyūkai cabinet is established, it will not last long. The Japanese military has a fundamental difference from the military of other countries, that is: the military's independence. For example, it can conduct diplomacy independently without going through the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Under the name of military secrecy, the military can directly report to the highest sovereign. As for the masses of the military, there are many "Zaikōgun" (reservist associations) and "Seinen Dan" (youth groups), and they have some influence on the small and medium-sized citizens. Therefore, in this "extraordinary time," whether the Seiyūkai wins or the Minseitō wins, they have to look at the military's face. As for the cabinet of decision, whether the Seiyūkai wins or the Minseitō wins, the cabinet candidates must have a close relationship with the military. If there is no close relationship, there is no possibility of a longer period of existence. If the number of seats in the Kokumin Dōmei increases, it indicates that "Japanism" is rising, and the "continental policy" will inevitably be strengthened, and the implementation of the military's will will be more based. However, as it currently appears, the number of seats in this faction will not exceed the Seiyūkai or the Minseitō. The high development of the Social Mass Party is currently impossible. Moreover, if there is considerable development, it will be differentiated and even suppressed, which is undoubtedly.

In short, it is still very depressing, as if a big storm is coming. The degree of depression is just like the economic status quo that seems to be prosperous but is not actually prosperous.

This decision, the result of the general election, can only show a further delineation of the battle lines in various layers. It is impossible to break through the depression. When the depression is broken through, it must be the advent of war. Now it is still in the stage of actively preparing for war.

(5)

The Italian-Ethiopian issue has not been resolved, the disarmament conference has failed, and Germany is demanding the return of colonies; during this period, Japan's demand that the powers recognize it as the center of stability in East Asia must be the best opportunity. According to reports, Soviet People's Commissar Molotov's speech stated that Japan and Germany have formed an alliance. Recently, Foreign Minister Hirota's speech, in addition to the so-called "three principles for China," also demanded that the Soviet Union withdraw the troops that have been increased in the Far East in recent years; in addition to military affairs, he also advocated free trade and opposed trade restrictions in various countries. This proposition of free trade shows that in today's recession, Japan's production index has already moved upward. It is also for this reason that its foreign policy dares to be tough. For these two reasons, the election of this decision, all factions naturally use "national defense" and "industry" as political slogans.

Japan is currently in the transition of military, political, and economic control and development, and this election is enough to show a further step forward. At the same time, the essence of the forces in each layer has gradually emerged. (End)

Two Bandit Leaders in Southwestern Fujian, Wu Dun, Executed by Firing Squad 78

——Du Shigong Sentenced to Ten Years of Imprisonment——

Xiamen Correspondence: Wu Sheng, a bandit leader in western Fujian, the pseudo-member of the Southwestern Fujian Military Commission and the pseudo-commander of the 9th Regiment, Guo Yiwei, the pseudo-member of the Military Commission and the pseudo-Minister of Party Affairs, and Du Shigong, the pseudo-member of the Central Military Commission and the pseudo-Chief of Staff of the Southwestern Fujian Military Commission, were successively captured in Fanshuikou, Yongding, in January. Du surrendered and wrote a letter of repentance, narrating the internal situation of the bandits. After the Longyan Second District Pacification Command inquired and reported to the Pacification Commissioner's Office in Fujian, it was requested to handle it. An order was received to sentence the two bandits Wu and Guo to death, and Du was sentenced to ten years of imprisonment. The two bandits Wu and Guo were then executed by firing squad in Longyan on January 22nd, and the Second District Pacification Command announced the crimes of the two bandits as follows: "According to Ma Shuming, the commander of the 56th Regiment of the 10th Division, who escorted the captured bandit leaders Wu Sheng, Guo Yiwei, and Du Shigong to the department, after inquiring, Wu Sheng was a member of the pseudo-Southwestern Fujian Military Commission and the pseudo-commander of the 9th Regiment, and Guo Yiwei was a member of the pseudo-Southwestern Fujian Military Commission and the pseudo-Minister of Party Affairs. Since their behavior is extremely obvious and their work is indeed determined, they shall be sentenced to death in accordance with Articles 1, 3, and 2 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Crimes Endangering the Republic of China. As for the name Du Shigong, although he is currently the Chief of Staff of the pseudo-Southwestern Fujian Military Commission, after investigation, his will has long been depressed, and he has been punished by the bandits for disagreement, and has even been expelled from the party once. When he was surrounded at Shuikoushan in Yongding, he was the first to sing that he was willing to surrender. Later, he wrote a letter of repentance, exposing the various conspiracies and tricks of the bandits, and his determination to oppose the Communists. He had already realized this, unlike the bandits such as Wu and Guo who were lost and did not know how to return. According to the law, he was sentenced to a reduced term of ten years of imprisonment, and the case was presented to Chiang, the Pacification Commissioner in Fujian, for instructions on the 14th of this month. Now, we have received Hao Wei's telegram stating that the captured bandit leaders Wu Sheng and Guo Yiwei have been sentenced to death, and Shi Shigong has been sentenced to ten years of imprisonment, all of which are approved and shall be executed separately. This is announced to show a warning, including the execution of one bandit leader Wu Sheng, a native of Yongding, Fujian, 25 years old, and Guo Yiwei, a native of Shanghang, Fujian, 26 years old." Liu Guitang Flees to Wu'an 80

Attacks and Occupies the Town, Causing Severe Harm

Henan Authorities Dispatch Troops to Strictly Defend

Kaifeng Correspondence: Liu Guitang's bandit troops, in Luochuan, which is under the jurisdiction of Shunde in Hebei Province, were severely attacked by Lin Zuozhen's regiment of Shang Zhen's troops, and then fled southwest to Huoshui, which is under the jurisdiction of Wu'an in northern Henan. They were again attacked by Zhang Xiaoyuan's regiment of Shang's troops, who advanced westward from Yueshantou, and Sun Dingchao's regiment, who advanced northwestward from Wu'an. Fearing being surrounded on three sides, the bandits fled northwestward again on the evening of the 27th. On the 28th, they retreated from Datong and Houzhang Village, northwest of Wu'an, to the area of Shahejin, Jianzishui, and Motou. Shang Zhen's troops are still tracking and pursuing them. At the same time, the Henan Provincial Authorities dispatched Tang Junde's unit of the 95th Division to garrison Linxian and Shexian counties. The 5th and 14th Security Regiments garrisoned the Daqing Road to strictly guard the money. On the 29th, according to a telegram from Zhangde, Liu's bandit troops of 500 people had captured Yicheng Town, northeast of Wu'an, causing severe harassment. It is recalled that when Liu's bandits fled to Henan in the 22nd year, they first went to Wu'an and Shexian counties, and then crossed the river from Mengxian County, causing harm to 65 counties in Henan Province. To this day, the general public still turns pale at the mention of it, so they all hope that the authorities will quickly quell it. (January 31st)

Songjiang Intensifies the Implementation of Self-Renewal Registration 81

The county government has recently ordered the district chiefs to investigate the self-renewal registration of opium smokers. Although it has exceeded 2,000 people, it is feared that there are still many omissions. Once the general inspection period arrives, unlicensed opium smokers will be punished, which is contrary to the government's intention of prudent imprisonment and compassionate sentencing. Therefore, yesterday, the county government convened a meeting of district chiefs and armed agencies to discuss effective methods of investigation. It was decided that starting from the 3rd, armed teams will be assigned to conduct simultaneous investigations by district. Ren Yingcang, the anti-opium commissioner specially dispatched by the Department of Civil Affairs, attended the meeting to declare the measures to promote the self-renewal registration of opium smokers. The district chiefs returned to their districts on the 2nd to convene township heads to strive to promote self-renewal registration. The situation is very tense. The county government also dispatched personnel to the districts to supervise. With such unity from top to bottom, unlicensed opium smokers can be cleared up, which is beneficial to the future of opium suppression.

Investigation of a Murder Case in Fanbang Township, Fengjing 82

Yao Cheng, a villager from Fanbang Township, Fengjing, who was nearly sixty years old, had one wife and one concubine. His wife, Cheng, was from Qingliang Nunnery. The couple's relationship was usually ordinary. On the morning of the second day of the new year, Cheng poured ash from the stove into the car shed. The embers reignited and burned three teeth of the car. The couple had an argument. Cheng, in a moment of anger, secretly swallowed ash and committed suicide. The Procuratorate received a letter from Ye Liuqiao and four other citizens of Qingliang Nunnery reporting a murder. The office immediately sent the chief bailiff Xue Bingzhang to the countryside to investigate. There was no Ye Liuqiao, and it was found that the above-mentioned situation had been reported. The office, considering that the case concerned a human life, specially sent prosecutor Lu Qi to the countryside for inspection.

Suzhou: Business Groups in Various Counties Reorganized Simultaneously 83

The Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Business Associations, in order to reorganize the business groups in various counties as ordered, will uniformly reorganize them into security teams in the counties on the 10th of this month. A joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees will be held in Yangzhou today (the 3rd) to discuss the follow-up issues of the business groups. Cheng Ganqing, the chairman of the Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce, went to Yangzhou on the 2nd to attend the meeting.

Yangzhou: Court Handles Real Estate Registration 84

Luo Zhi, the president of the Jiangdu District Court, believes that real estate registration is the only way to protect the private rights of the people and prevent unnecessary litigation. In all modern countries ruled by law, the source of litigation can be clarified and the trial can be facilitated, mostly because of the remarkable effectiveness of the registration system. In the eleventh year of the Republic of China, there was already the promulgation of the Real Estate Registration Ordinance. In provinces where it was implemented in accordance with the regulations, the people felt convenient. However, in Jiangdu, the registration has not been carried out due to the imperfect organization of the court, which has made the people's private rights lack definite protection, made investigation difficult in civil litigation, and made lawsuits over objections to enforcement frequently appear. The request for filing is also just a cover-up. He specially reported to the High Court and instructed the court to establish a real estate registration office in accordance with the law to carry out registration, so as to rectify the origin and clarify the source. It has now started working on the 1st, and announced to the public that those with land rights should come to the court to register and receive certificates.

Nantong: Preventing Disputes over Tax Police Searching for Salt 85

In various counties under Nantong, due to the tax police searching for smuggled salt among the people, major disputes have repeatedly arisen. The Nantong District Commissioner's Office, after discussing with the county heads of Tong, Ru, Hai, Chong, Qi, and Jing, telegraphed the provincial government to consult the Ministry of Finance to stop it. The Ministry of Finance, according to the Salt Affairs Audit Office, has formulated eight measures for tax police to check salt, stipulating that searches should be carried out after sunrise and before sunset, and should be handled in conjunction with local administrative agency personnel.

Zhang Xiaoruo's Concubine Dies of Serious Injuries 86

Zhang Xiaoruo was attacked by thugs in Shanghai, and his concubine, Li Fuchu, was also injured. At the end of last year, she was transferred to Nantong for treatment, but died of her injuries yesterday at the Nantong Hospital, and was buried in a coffin in Dongsi.

Hangzhou: Borrowing Money to Complete the Jiahu Highway 87

In order to complete the Jiahu Highway within a limited time, the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau specially sent Deputy Director Li Yu and Accounting Section Chief Bao Jiling to visit Jin Runquan, the manager of the Bank of China, to discuss borrowing 100,000 yuan to meet the needs of the project, so as not to cause it to stop. The funds will be gradually allocated by the Department of Finance in the future.

Civil Servants Provide Labor Service 88

On the 2nd, civil servants from various agencies in the provincial capital continued to provide labor service during their holidays, participating in dredging the Yunsi River at Taotian. More than 1,200 people participated, which was extremely lively.

After Reading the "Central Disaster Relief Organization Policy" 89

— Duanyuan

Since the Yangtze River flood in the twentieth year of the Republic, major water and drought disasters have succeeded each other continuously. The central government has mobilized to respond tirelessly, and the funds allocated have reached tens of millions of yuan. Judging from historical records, the disaster relief policies of past dynasties may not have surpassed our government's, which is what our government can tell the people with satisfaction. However, relief administration differs in its nature and methods from other government affairs, and the establishment of a specialized department is still in its infancy in our country's political system. The efforts of the past have been recognized by the people of the country, and the effectiveness of the future should be improved. Yesterday, this newspaper published Consultant Baker's "Central Disaster Relief Organization Policy," which is based on his twenty years of experience in disaster relief in China. His words may be what people have not said, or what everyone can say, but it is different from the empty talk of those who simply follow ideals, and it has value for research and discussion. Now, I will discuss a few points with the readers.

1. Methods of Providing Relief 90

The current method of providing relief is to investigate first and then release. After the investigation and release personnel arrive in a county with the funds, they are instructed by the local administrative personnel to prepare a register of disaster victims, which is reported from the district to the county, and then collected by the county. After the investigation and release personnel receive the register, they conduct a household-by-household review of the register, and at the same time issue relief tickets. They select a date and location, and the disaster victims hold the tickets to receive relief. After this procedure is completed, the relief funds enter the hands of the disaster victims. It takes a short time to dispatch the investigation and release personnel, remit the relief funds, and transport the relief goods. However, the preparation of the register and the review of the register take a lot of time. According to past experience, in places with convenient transportation, it cannot be completed in two or three months, let alone in other places with blocked transportation. However, the register is not accurate, and the review may be obscured. Recently, newspapers and magazines, in short stories about rural disaster relief, often have quite unforgiving expressions regarding the fairness and timeliness of the current method. This is a general and honest reaction, and those who handle relief should pay serious attention and seek improvement in methods. The work-relief method mentioned by Mr. Baker can be recognized as a more time-saving and fair method. It can avoid the complexity of investigation and its malpractices, and in addition to saving lives, it can also have the positive effect of construction. In the future, it should be adopted as much as possible to replace the old method of emergency relief. However, this kind of work-relief plan must be planned in advance, so that it can be implemented immediately after a disaster occurs. It is by no means the so-called work-relief that is currently available, but after the disaster occurs, the available funds are allocated, and then the survey and design are carried out, and workers are called to implement it. Not only does it take longer than emergency relief, but also the recruitment of foreign workers leads to the suspicion of disturbing farmers. The work-relief mentioned by Mr. Baker, in my opinion, should be that the central and local construction agencies pre-approve the construction projects to be carried out in various places in the next three or four years, and make budgets. If there is a bumper year, then workers will be conscripted or urged to complete them in order. If there is a famine year, then work can be started in advance according to the order, and the disaster can be completed by labor. If this is the case, then the country has a construction budget of one yuan, which is a disaster relief budget of one yuan. Disaster relief can promote construction, and construction can relieve disaster at the same time. This is why work-relief is preferable.

2. The Allocation of Relief Funds 91

The final distribution of relief funds is executed by the investigation and release personnel. If the investigation and release personnel lack the ability, or for various public and private reasons, they do not release the funds, or they do not release them in the right way or at the right time, then the value of that part of the relief funds is lost. Therefore, if the allocation of relief funds is to be appropriate and the utilization is to be flexible, the central agency, whether it is a government agency or a people's organization, should have the power to control and supervise the relief funds from beginning to end. The entire amount of relief funds should not be allocated at once after distribution, but should be allocated for each use to achieve the function of jurisdiction and adjustment. Mr. Baker's proposal is based on experience and is based on the fact that it has always been easy for various groups and agencies to allocate relief funds, but it is difficult to settle accounts, and it is often delayed for more than two or three years. This is why rumors arise and trust is lost. Mr. Baker's method, in short, is the fixed-amount revolving fund system in accounting. Since this system has been implemented in various commercial and administrative agencies, I do not see why it cannot be adopted in the expenditure of relief funds as well.

Section 3: The Organization of the Highest Authority 92

The central highest authority, which presides over national revitalization affairs, bears a more significant administrative responsibility for China, a nation afflicted by numerous disasters, than any other institution. To fully leverage its functions and fulfill its duties, it must, of course, have adequate funding and specialized personnel as prerequisites. Although various ministries and commissions are tightening their belts due to today's financial constraints, this authority should be treated as a special case, given the pressing needs arising from our country's unique circumstances. However, the officials appointed to take charge should comprehend the gravity of their mission and approach the handover of duties with utmost solemnity, ensuring that public funds are not wasted. The general ills of Chinese administrative institutions are that nothing gets done due to a lack of funds, existing only as window dressing. Conversely, if funds are sufficient, they are busy accommodating superfluous personnel, still achieving nothing. It is hoped that such a state of affairs will not manifest in the revitalization administrative authority. Considering the close relationship between revitalization and other administrative aspects, the highest-ranking official should be appointed from among those who are advanced in years, possess high moral character and profound prestige, for the sake of administrative convenience. The members of its core staff must be selected based on their abilities, and its leaders should be staffed with dedicated individuals possessing rich disaster relief experience, enthusiasm, knowledge, physical strength, the ability to endure hardship, the capacity for progress, diligence, fearlessness in the face of difficulty, and full commitment. Consultant Baker concluded that if China had competent revitalization leaders, its disaster relief capabilities would be no less than those of any country in the world. We firmly believe this.

Why Do We Study Mathematics? And How Do We Study Mathematics? (Part 1) Professor of Great China University 93

— Ren Mengxian

(Lecture to secondary school students nationwide on January 9th and 11th of the 25th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1936])

"Mathematics," as a discipline, has always been valued in schools—especially in secondary schools. Despite the considerable efforts of teachers and students, the performance, as seen in statistical reports, remains poor and, according to some, is the worst. Moreover, in recent years, the results of the high school entrance examinations in various provinces and cities, as well as the entrance examinations for various universities, consistently show mathematics as the weakest subject. What is the reason for this? Whose responsibility is it? The issues of provincial and municipal entrance examinations and university admissions are beyond the scope of this lecture; their merits and demerits should be discussed separately. If we focus solely on secondary schools themselves to investigate the reasons for the poor performance in mathematics and the responsibility for it, we can identify two aspects: teachers and students. I will now begin with what I wish to contribute to the students:

As far as I know, many students in certain secondary schools (in some schools, the majority) find mathematics uninteresting. Because it is uninteresting, they do not work hard; because they do not work hard, their performance worsens. Each school, every semester and school year, has a mathematics failure rate that often exceeds one-quarter. This has become a norm in calculating grades. But why are students not interested in mathematics? There are three explanations for this:

Some say that most students do not need to study mathematics. Because they do not feel the need, they are not interested. I believe that education must adapt to needs, which is certainly true. However, the question is, is there fundamentally no need, or is the need not being stimulated? You will understand as you hear more below.

Some say that not every student is capable of learning mathematics. Analyzing the minds of young people, some are inclined towards the humanities, others towards the sciences. It is inappropriate to force everyone to learn mathematics. I believe this reason is highly inadequate. We can say that every student may not become a mathematician, but to say that someone is born unable to learn mathematics is an unfounded assertion. Because the mathematics taught in secondary schools and even ordinary universities (excluding mathematics departments) is limited to the elementary level, as long as one grasps the process and advances step by step, it is not at all difficult. To say that one cannot learn even this much is unduly self-defeating.

Some say that even if students feel the need for mathematics and do not consider themselves unsuited to it, they still find mathematics troublesome and monotonous. I believe that trouble and monotony are unavoidable phenomena in life. We know that the universe is diverse, but from another perspective, it is also very monotonous. For example, the Earth revolves around the Sun, moving step by step, passing second by second. How monotonous is that! If it suddenly felt bored and stopped or sped up slightly, what would happen to the world?

According to these three explanations, students lack a strong interest in learning, which is indeed a reason for poor performance. However, the interest in learning can be cultivated. How to stimulate needs? How to shift individual biases? And how to develop habits? These are not unsolvable problems. Before presenting learning methods, I will first explain the purpose of studying mathematics.

First, studying mathematics can provide tools for scientific research. If we want to survive in the world in the future, we must study science; and the foundation of all sciences is built upon mathematics. The natural sciences in elementary school and the physics and chemistry in junior high school only explain the superficial aspects of natural phenomena and may not require the help of mathematics. However, in high school, one often needs to use arithmetic, algebra, geometry, and trigonometry to calculate problems in physics and chemistry. Such as the distance and time of movement; the composition and function of forces; the pressure and specific gravity of water and air; the absorption and release of heat and the expansion and contraction of objects; the progression of light and the propagation of waves; the strength of electric current and the magnitude of resistance; as well as calculations of atomic weight, molecular weight, periodic law, chemical equivalent, chemical equations, etc.—where is mathematics not needed? If we go further, any scientific book, if it is somewhat specialized, can be flipped open and one will see short d's, long s's, continuously recorded in lengthy passages. This is the most powerful and effective tool for science—calculus. Without calculus, the material civilization of the twentieth century would not have developed to its current level. But if we cannot learn arithmetic, algebra, geometry, and trigonometry, we cannot learn calculus, which means we cannot study science. Because mathematics is the stepping stone to studying science, mathematics is the science for studying science. The reason we find science so difficult is that our mathematical foundation is poor and our tools are incomplete. If one has a considerable cultivation of mathematics, one can gradually delve deeper, understand science, and reach the point of invention and creation to benefit society and humanity.

Second, studying mathematics can solve problems in daily life. In clothing, food, housing, transportation, production, consumption, whenever there is a quantitative relationship, we must apply mathematical knowledge to meet the needs of our interaction with the world. This is the most obvious, most intimate, and universally felt and encountered benefit, which I need not elaborate on.

Third, studying mathematics can guide the correct path of life. We can say that we do not hope to become mathematicians, do not plan to study science, and even say that we do not need the convenience of life, but we cannot say that we do not want to be human. Mathematics is also a philosophy that guides us on how to be human, because the characteristics of mathematics are often in direct opposition to various undesirable phenomena in society. To list a few:

Certainty vs. hypocrisy. Duplicity and inconsistency are more prevalent among those who claim to be civilized. Not only is this the case in a single society or nation, but an atmosphere of hypocrisy pervades the entire world. This disease can be cured with mathematics, because mathematics is absolutely certain and never lies. For example, one cannot be less than zero, and two plus three cannot equal four or six.

Strictness vs. sloppiness. Perfunctoriness and casualness are common attitudes, and "close enough" has become a catchphrase. This disease can also be cured with mathematics, because mathematics is very strict and never allows for carelessness. For example, can one be careless or casual when proving geometric theorems?

Order vs. disorder. People usually allow time and space to be inverted and disordered. Public gatherings are even more chaotic and disturbing. To remedy such chaotic phenomena, one can borrow the function of mathematics. Because mathematics is the most orderly, making a diagram or writing an equation requires following a specific procedure, arranging things neatly from front to back, left to right. If society could be like this, there would be no conflict.

Universality vs. exceptionalism. In other countries, only foreign guests representing their nations can enjoy the convenience of extraterritoriality. In our country, there are often people who enjoy preferential treatment outside the law. This special situation is most detrimental to the progress and unity of society and the nation. Recently, our enemies have used the pretext that a certain province has a special environment and a certain place requires special measures to oppress us. However, mathematics has no exceptions under a certain regulation. So-called universality is one of the characteristics of mathematics. With this training, there will be no drawbacks from claiming exceptions.

Broad and precise vs. narrowness. Narrowness is a trait of people, because they have not studied solid geometry, or have studied it and have already forgotten it. Therefore, they lack a spatial concept, fighting desperately in the horns of a bull. Negligence is also a common state of people, because they have not learned precise algorithms. Therefore, they are careless and superficial, easily giving up, causing many mistakes. If we use mathematics to correct them, they will look up, broaden their horizons, become more meticulous, and become more peaceful.

I have said above that the reason students' interest in learning mathematics is not strong is because they are afraid of difficulty. Mathematics is indeed not an easy subject, but at the elementary level, this is not yet the case. Many problems, usually considered difficult, such as the application of four arithmetic operations and the initial proofs in geometry, have few methods and theorems that can be cited, making it difficult to obtain explanations that are exactly relevant to the problem. Another example is solving simultaneous quadratic equations and proving trigonometric and inverse trigonometric function identities, which require many steps and are difficult to reach the final step. In fact, these types of problems are just sometimes too simple, sometimes more complex, but not difficult. Because they are ultimately not impossible, not unsolvable, like the loci that cannot be constructed in elementary geometry or algebraic equations above the fifth degree, those are truly difficult problems! Also, it is natural to feel difficult when teaching trigonometry and analytical geometry to someone who has never studied any geometry. If you follow the order from the first year of junior high school to the third year of high school, step by step, what difficulty is there? Therefore, scholars only need to pay attention to the following three points in their actual learning, and there will be no so-called difficulty.

Theory must be concise. A discipline, or a part of it, always has a theory on which it is based, and each must have its center of argument. Although elementary mathematics is very simple, it also has simple theories. But if you can grasp the key points, the rest will be easily solved and will not be a problem. For example, the solution of algebraic equations is based on the principle of "gradually finding equivalent equations of the original equation"; the most important thing in analytical geometry is the theorem that "points whose coordinates are the roots of the equation are all on the locus represented by the equation, and any point taken on the locus, its coordinates are all suitable for the equation"; as long as these key points are truly recognized, appropriately summarized, and grasped, they can be applied infinitely.

The system must be clear. Scientific methods value classification. Although the content may be mixed and the conditions may be numerous, each has its system and the possibility of classes. The most clearly structured in mathematics is geometry, with one theorem, one definition, extending one by one, allowing no disorder. Another example is that numbers in algebra can be interpreted as generalized arithmetic numbers, so various algorithms in algebra can be regarded as extensions of arithmetic; and the establishment of the number system gradually expands from integers and fractions to irrational numbers and imaginary numbers, thus combining into the large range of complex numbers. All of these are very orderly and meaningful connections in mathematics. If scholars can distinguish them clearly, they will not feel complex.

Basic methods must be proficient. Studying mathematics is not only about understanding, but also about proficiency. As explained earlier, many principles and methods come from the shallow to the deep, layered and tortuous, so you must start from the very first step, practice step by step, and become proficient in the whole body. Students who fail algebra and trigonometry do not fail because they do not understand the theory of algebra and trigonometry, but because they are not familiar with the calculation of numbers, so the answer has no result; analytical geometry cannot be tested, not because the properties of the quadric curve are not clear, nor because the method of graphing is not known, but because the algebraic equations cannot be organized, the geometric theorems cannot be applied, and the trigonometric formulas cannot be manipulated freely; any teacher who has looked at the test paper can point out the students' shortcomings. Therefore, when we study mathematics, we should pay attention to practice, and even more should pay attention to basic practice.

As for some problems that are not difficult, but are inevitably complicated, this is undeniable. But if we acknowledge the importance of science, we must cultivate people who are proficient in science, so we must train minds that are suitable for science and spirits that are in line with science. This attitude and habit of not being afraid of trouble, being patient, being diligent, burying one's head in hard work, can be deeply cultivated and actively tempered when studying mathematics, so as to be prepared to undertake more complex and difficult work in the future. What is the complexity of mathematical formulas?

Ladies and gentlemen! The vast natural world and the brilliant academic world have yet to be explored and developed by us. Do not belittle yourselves. Hurry up and work hard. Who knows if you will become an inventor in the future? Is it impossible to make contributions in mathematics and bring great light to mankind? As long as you are not afraid of difficulties, do not settle for ease, raise unlimited interest, make a very big determination, and you can always achieve your goals and benefit the world! Archimedes was studying geometry when enemy soldiers had already arrived at the window, yet he was still thinking deeply without stopping. This is the true spirit of studying mathematics, and the best way to achieve the greatest purpose of studying mathematics.

In short, studying mathematics can correct various bad habits in society; it can guide our view of life; although achieving this goal is not the function of mathematics itself, it cannot but be considered a good prescription for saving the dying customs.

Now that the purpose is clear, we can discuss methods. How do we study mathematics, or rather, how do we make our mathematics performance good? Teachers certainly have a great responsibility; but teachers can only find ways to stimulate students' interest in mathematics based on their goals of learning mathematics, and find ways to guide them to work hard. For example, if a child cannot walk, adults can only lead them to walk, not walk for them. Whether mathematics performance is good or not still depends on whether the students themselves work hard or not. So today my point of view focuses on the students' side.

Current students can be divided into five levels, and those who are unwilling to work hard and have no awareness are not included. The last level of these five levels is the students who only wake up after failing the exam, but do not know how to mend the fold after the sheep is lost, and do not hurry to think of remedial methods, but only know how to argue with the teacher about the score; the fourth level is the students who know their past mistakes after failing the exam and study hard; although his hard work is too late, but it is already much better than the last level!

Issuance of Consolidated and Reconstruction Bonds Receives Positive Response from Various Sectors 94

Old Bonds to be Withdrawn and Exchanged Once New Bonds are Printed

Shanghai Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange Decides to Temporarily Suspend Auctions

Sound Financial System with Eight Major Banks Completed

According to the New Sound News Agency, after the Ministry of Finance issued 146 million yuan of Consolidated Bonds and 34 million yuan of Reconstruction Bonds on February 1st, the Shanghai Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange temporarily suspended auctions. Once the new bonds are printed, the old bonds will be withdrawn and exchanged, while simultaneously promoting a sound financial system and supporting production and construction. Details are as follows:

Withdrawal of Old Bonds and Exchange for New Bonds

After the issuance of 146 million yuan of Consolidated Bonds on February 1st, the National Public Bond Holders Association first issued a declaration of support. Now the Ministry of Finance has expedited the printing of the Consolidated Bonds. Once printing is completed, the following categories will be withdrawn: (A) six types including the 22nd Year Patriotic Treasury Bonds; (B) five types including the 19th Year Rehabilitation Treasury Bonds; (C) nine types including the 18th Year Disbandment Treasury Bonds; (D) eight types including the 19th Year Customs Bonds; and (E) five types including the 22nd Year Customs Treasury Bonds. Old bonds will be withdrawn and exchanged for new bonds.

Securities Trading Temporarily Suspended

Since the Ministry of Finance sent Xu Zhichu and others to supervise the delivery of securities at the Shanghai Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange and stipulated that, regardless of new or old transactions, sellers must provide the actual goods to be stored at the Central Trust Bureau, the Brokers Association convened a meeting to request a remedy. The Exchange received an order from the Ministry of Finance to temporarily suspend trading until the investigation of speculation and manipulation is completed. Although yesterday was Sunday and a day of rest, it is said that the Exchange has decided to temporarily suspend auctions. The date of resumption will depend on the order of the Ministry of Finance.

Principal Redemption Every Six Months

The 16th principal redemption of the first tranche of the 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds, the 7th principal redemption of the 7% Treasury Bonds, and the 7th principal redemption of the 6% Treasury Bonds were announced by the Ministry of Finance in Announcement No. 128 on January 27th, stipulating that the lottery for principal redemption would be held at the Shanghai Banking Association on February 10th. The Banking and Currency Exchange Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce were instructed to send personnel to supervise. Now, because the above three types of bonds have been merged into the Consolidated Bonds, the 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds as Category D, and the 6% and 7% Treasury Bonds as Category E, the planned lottery for principal redemption on February 10th will be temporarily suspended. It is noted that the Consolidated Bonds stipulate that principal and interest will be redeemed by lottery every six months.

Sound System to Support Production

To complete the legal currency policy, establish a sound financial system, support production and construction, balance national treasury revenue and expenditure, and stabilize the bond market fund, after the Ministry of Finance issued 34 million yuan of Reconstruction Bonds on February 1st, the Ministry of Finance has actively proceeded with the above-mentioned designated uses. Such as completing the eight major banks, reorganizing the Central Bank into a reserve bank, becoming a bank of banks, and establishing a real estate bank, etc., scheduled to be realized one by one before the end of this year.

Various Industries Support the Policy

According to the New Sound News Agency reporter, investigations from major industries yesterday revealed that China's industry and commerce have been severely affected by the global recession, resulting in unusual decline. Since the Ministry of Finance implemented the new currency system policy on November 4th last year, there has been no concern about a lack of currency in the market, and various industries have been invigorated. The difficult hurdle of the general conclusion of 1935 has also been safely overcome. Now the government's issuance of Reconstruction Bonds, the establishment of a sound financial system, and support for production are the only appropriate measures. It is said that endorsements will be declared one after another. The revival of agriculture, industry, and commerce can also be foreseen.

Minister Kong to Report to Capital Tonight

After Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi discussed with leaders of the financial and industrial and commercial sectors in Shanghai and the Public Bond Holders Association the issuance of the Consolidated Bonds and Reconstruction Bonds, it is said that he is scheduled to take the Shanghai-Nanjing night express train to the capital tonight to attend the Executive Yuan's regular meeting on Tuesday to report on the handling of the bond cases.

Silver Trade to Convene National Delegates' Meeting 99

Discussing the Purity of Silver Ornaments

The Shanghai Silver Trade Guild held a members' meeting at its premises at 2 PM on the first day of the month (yesterday). Present were all the executive committee members Ying Xiansan, Fu Shengmao, Fei Zushou, Kong Lanfang, Xu Zhifang, Yao Guiqing, and more than twenty member representatives including Yan Zhiyun, Lin Xiaoyu, and Yu Yongsui. The meeting was chaired by Fu Shengmao. The chairman reported that the guild received a directive from the Ministry of Finance on the 23rd of last month (the last day of the lunar year), regarding the requested "Regulations for the Management of Silver Products," altering certain provisions. Members were immediately notified that very night. However, due to the general business closure for the holidays, a meeting could not be convened. The chairman consulted with members yesterday and found them deeply anxious and fearful. The only recourse is to submit another request to the Ministry of Finance, seeking approval to adhere to the exception clause in Article 11 of the Management Regulations.

A certain shop replaced a silver cup with the "Yang Qinghe" brand with one made of copper. The police brought a public prosecution, and the First Special District Court ruled against them. The guild has entrusted legal counsel, Lawyer Xi Yuchang, to publish a notice, advising all sectors to be cautious when commissioning silver articles, especially if they are not refurbished or re-decorated by silver shops. Mr. Gu Suming, the chief representative of the Zhejiang Province Silver Trade, sent a letter yesterday, stating he will arrive in Shanghai tomorrow, intending to jointly initiate a call with this guild to gather representatives from all gold and silver factions nationwide to come to Shanghai for discussions, and make a large-scale petition. After the report, Fu continued to express his views, stating in brief: The Ministry of Finance's directive states that various countries now use chemical silver, but national customs differ between East and West. Foreign production uses machines and electricity, while our country uses lamps, bellows, hands, and brains. Learning begins in childhood and continues into old age. Changes in patterns are determined by the needs of the times. This refers to workmanship. When foreigners purchase utensils and ornaments, they discard them once they are old or broken. In our country, social customs value the quality of silver ornaments and utensils, using them for savings. When funds are needed, these ornaments are pawned. Therefore, buyers first inquire about the regular price and are unwilling to simply discard them. This refers to the psychology and customs of our society. Our trade has always used pure silver. Once it is changed to 30% silver, shops will lack electric machinery, and craftsmen's skills will be useless. Furthermore, jewelry cannot be made with 30% silver. After repeated consideration, jewelry must still be made of pure silver, but the sales volume is extremely small. However, interior traders mainly still use ornaments. The lowest quality utensils can be made with 70% silver, which would not be too difficult for workmanship. If 30% silver is used, I can assert that no one will care, and livelihoods will be driven to the brink of ruin. The Ministry of Finance preserves silver to maintain our country's economic lifeline, and its intentions are good. However, the amount of ornaments scattered among the people is limited. When the nation faces danger, every citizen will surely remove their hairpins and earrings to assist the country's urgent needs. The Italian people's aid to the national treasury has earned worldwide acclaim. Our people's patriotism is no less. I believe the Ministry of Finance will not cause millions of law-abiding workers to face unemployment, and so on. In the end, the third submission will be handled by the chairman with full authority, but it must be done quickly. Once completed, it should be directly submitted to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce for forwarding to the Ministry of Finance.

The organization of a national gold and silver trade joint petition group will wait until the Zhejiang Province representative arrives in Shanghai, after which detailed discussions will be held to decide the next course of action.

Austerity Measures 103

A reporter from Xin Sheng News learned from money traders yesterday that the money trade has been affected by the overall recession, resulting in most firms' profits being only around 50,000 yuan at most, with half of the industry barely breaking even. This year, they have unanimously adopted austerity measures, being particularly cautious with overdrafts, requiring reliable guarantors before granting credit. The annual meeting will be held on February 5th at the Inner Garden in the South City and on February 10th at the Money Trade Guild Hall in the North City. In addition to reporting on the meeting and paying respects to deceased elders, they will also discuss new business strategies. The Money Trade Joint Reserve Treasury has been quite effective since its establishment, with ample reserves. To save expenses, the assembly passed a resolution to return the old site at the mouth of Xingren Lane on Ningbo Road, and move to the hall downstairs in the Money Trade Guild building on Shanxi Road East on Ningbo Road, which is the Money Trade Market. Workers have been hired to renovate the space, and they will move in as soon as the work is completed.
