Discussion of the Promotion of National Products by the National Products Community 105

The Business Is Seeing Development

The Future Is Quite Promising

Discussion by Standing Committee Member Pan 106

Xin Xin News reports that the National Products Movement Joint Association, organized by various groups in this city, has been actively promoting national products since its establishment on the 10th of last month, dividing its efforts into domestic and international departments. A reporter from Xin Xin News visited Mr. Pan Yangyao, a standing committee member of the association, yesterday, who provided detailed information about the work situation, which is summarized as follows:

Active Implementation 107

According to Mr. Pan, promoting national products is currently essential. Therefore, in recent years, many have been actively advocating for it. Since the National Products Year for Women and Students was held successively, there has been considerable success in promoting national products. Looking at the fact that the major factories in this city have safely survived two major New Year closures in the midst of a global recession, and that the customs bureau announced a surplus of five million yuan in December last year, it is evident that the public's love for national products is considerable. If manufacturers can continuously improve their products, and society continues to vigorously promote them, the future of national products is immeasurable. To ensure effectiveness, the association has drafted a general outline of a work plan and is actively implementing it.

Domestic Work 108

After the joint meeting of the domestic departments decided to focus on the Yangtze River area, the director of the department, Wang Xingyao, drafted a work outline, deciding to start with propaganda and actively organize a propaganda team to set off in three groups, each group consisting of three or four people, to conduct propaganda in Nanjing, Wuhu, Bengbu, Anqing, Jiujiang, Changsha, Hankou, Yichang, Wanxian, Chongqing, and other places, and to discuss the consumption and promotion of national products. The director of the General Affairs Department, Wang Renzhi, and his party set off the night before last.

Overseas Work 109

After deciding to focus on Southeast Asia, the international department, under the direction of the director Zhang Huikang, formulated a work plan, deciding to start with a needs assessment and organize a Southeast Asia exploration team to explore the islands of Southeast Asia and Malaya, and to request the assistance of local embassies to achieve twice the result with half the effort. At the same time, a publication will be launched to facilitate propaganda. It is planned that these measures will be implemented separately after convening a meeting of the heads of the departments next week.

Discussion by Director Wang 110

Zhong Yang News reports that the National Products business has been developing rapidly in recent years, and efforts to promote national products have been spared. The National Products Introduction Center, jointly established by major manufacturers in this city, has established national product companies all over the country. After the first establishment in Shanghai, it gradually spread to remote provinces. As of the end of last year, there were eight established locations, including Fuzhou and Xijing. One location in Chongqing has been in operation for half a year, but due to the construction of buildings, it only officially opened this year. According to the reporter's inquiry, the operating conditions in various locations are as follows:

Conditions in Various Locations 111

Last year, the National Products Companies operating year-round in various locations included five places: Fuzhou, Zhenjiang, Zhengzhou, Wenzhou, and Changsha. Jinan was established in late April. According to the company's office survey, the total operating income of various companies throughout the year reached more than 1,922,800 yuan, of which Changsha had the most, reaching more than 460,000 yuan, followed by Wenzhou, with more than 380,000 yuan, and Zhenjiang, with more than 230,000 yuan. Although Xijing only operated for seven months, it also reached more than 140,000 yuan, which shows the people's love for national products in various places.

Social Demand 112

According to the Director Wang from the office told the reporter, the situation of promoting national products in various places is quite optimistic. However, the inland people are simple and honest, and their clothes are mostly cloth and fine silk crepe, accounting for more than 50% of the total sales. Other daily necessities are also mostly simple and unadorned. Therefore, it is necessary to deeply understand the social needs and select and match goods according to the local conditions, so it is quite popular with customers.

Planned Establishment 113

Director Wang also mentioned that there are more than 50 companies planned to be established, but only one-fifth of them have been established. Therefore, we still need to continue our efforts. Currently, Kunming and Guangzhou are building buildings, and they should be established within the year. In the past, the establishment of companies in various places was in response to the proposals of local gentry and merchants, and the agreement was carried out. Now, the board of directors has decided that the office will consult with local people on the establishment according to the needs of various places, and plans to build companies in the nearby neighboring cities of the existing companies in order to promote them.

Food Industry Leader Gu Xinyi Talks About the Effectiveness of Transportation and Sales Control 114

Last Year, Foreign Rice Imports Reached 10 Million Yuan

The Ministry of Finance's Large Warehouse in Jiujiang Has Been Implemented

A reporter from Xin Sheng News met with Gu Shengyi, a leader in the food industry in this city. According to him, foreign rice imports last year reached a staggering 10 million yuan. Our country is established on agriculture, and yet this phenomenon exists. It is not only shocking, but also shameful. Since the Ministry of Finance established the Food Transportation and Sales Administration and implemented control over food transportation and sales, it has achieved great results. Foreign rice imports have gradually decreased. This can be proved by the fact that there were no records of foreign rice imports in January this year. The large warehouse established by the Ministry of Finance in Jiujiang has also been implemented. Furthermore, because the central government has the determination to rescue the rural areas, and the financial community has implemented many rural loans, the rural areas are expected to recover. Furthermore, with proper control over food transportation and sales, the problem of food self-sufficiency in our country is expected to be solved.

Strong Exports Tung Oil Urgently Needs Improvement 116

Improve Production, Manufacturing, Transportation, and Sales to Establish International Reputation

Strive for Direct Trade to Consolidate Overseas Markets

This year, our country's tung oil exports are extremely strong, which is rare in recent years. This is indeed a somewhat optimistic phenomenon in our country's foreign trade. However, when considering the reasons for the sudden increase in exports, it is purely due to a temporary surge in foreign demand, rather than our country's tung oil having the ability to promote sales. If we want to maintain the permanent prosperity of tung oil exports, we still need to fundamentally improve the production and sales of tung oil. A reporter from Xin Xin News specially explored and recorded the reasons for the prosperity of tung oil exports and the areas that urgently need improvement, as follows:

Reasons for Prosperity 117

From January to September last year, our country's tung oil exports increased sharply. The total export volume for nine months was 576,987 hectoliters, an increase of 7.4% compared with the same period last year. The total export value was 29,938,098 yuan, an increase of 41% compared with the same period last year. The average price per hectoliter was 51.8 yuan, an increase of 12.5 yuan compared with 39.3 yuan in the same period last year. The prosperity of its exports is rare in recent years. The reasons for the increase in our country's tung oil exports and the increase in prices last year are as follows:

* The United States is our country's largest sales market for tung oil. The average annual import reaches 120 million pounds. After the economic panic occurred, it was reduced to 70 to 80 million pounds. In recent years, due to the implementation of the economic recovery plan, it has been quite successful. Various industries are gradually recovering, and the demand for tung oil is gradually returning to normal. Therefore, our country's tung oil sales in the United States have also increased.

* After the Italo-Abyssinian War broke out, Mediterranean traffic was often in danger of being blocked. European countries, in order to plan ahead, are actively preparing raw materials, and tung oil is one of the important raw materials, so the demand has increased even more.

* Our country's tung oil production is scattered in the inland, and the transportation and sales of goods are quite troublesome. Once the demand increases sharply, the market inventory is exhausted, and it cannot be supplied continuously, so the price increases accordingly.

Should Be Improved 118

In summary, it can be seen that the prosperity of our country's tung oil exports last year was mainly due to the sharp increase in overseas demand, and the increase in its price was due to the fact that our country's tung oil supply could not meet demand. Therefore, although our country's tung oil exports were very prosperous last year, this phenomenon is only the result of a temporary shortage of supply, and it does not mean that our country's tung oil has gained the ability to promote sales in overseas markets. It is difficult to regard it as a normal development. Therefore, if we want to maintain the permanent prosperity of tung oil exports, we still need to fundamentally improve the production and sales of tung oil. The most important points are the following five:

* Our country's tung oil cultivation methods are not requested.

* After the households purchase it, they store it at will, which is prone to rotting. The oil extraction method is also very outdated, so the quality is poor, the color is uneven, the impurities cannot be removed cleanly, the oil residue is too heavy, and the acidity is too high. Furthermore, because oil extraction is a handicraft industry, it is difficult to have a uniform quality.

* Our country's oil extraction sticks to the old methods, so the oil extraction rate is extremely low. The amount of oil lost every year in the country is alarming.

* The transportation and sales procedures are extremely complicated. Some merchants mix adulterated oil to make huge profits, which deteriorates the quality and affects foreign credit. Recently, the Commodity Inspection Bureaus of various ports have formulated合格qualified standards, but the standards set are lower than those in the United States. This should be gradually increased.

* Poor loading and transportation methods, high freight rates, and frequent blockages often prevent timely delivery, so the market is at risk of being unable to meet demand.

* Tung oil exports are purely controlled by foreign firms. There are no domestic organizations directly engaged in tung oil exports, and oil merchants cannot communicate, so the market price is purely manipulated by foreigners.

Consolidate the Market 119

Tung oil is one of our country's special products and has a monopolistic nature in the international market. Although the United States is also engaged in tung planting, it is currently far from being self-sufficient. If we can seize the opportunity to improve and establish international credibility, the future will be very bright. The most important way to improve is in production, manufacturing, transportation, and sales. In terms of production, we should first concentrate our country's tung planting, with the government's help, to engage in large-scale planting. Such scientific methods can be cited, the variety can be uniform, the production volume can be calculated, and production can be increased. In terms of manufacturing, new methods should be actively adopted for oil extraction, so that the oil extraction rate can be increased. At the same time, we must pay attention to refining and grading the oil, and determine the standards for each grade. In terms of transportation, we should research economic loading and transportation methods, and transportation organizations should also find ways to reduce freight rates and implement responsible transportation to achieve economic and convenient purposes. As for trade, the fundamental plan is to concentrate exports. If domestic tung oil merchants can unite and form a large-scale export organization with a common force, our country's overseas tung oil market can be consolidated day by day.

Ministry of Industry Orders Social Bureau to Improve Cooperative Organization 123

Promulgation of a Concise Table of Registration Methods

According to Shen Shi News Agency, the Ministry of Industry states that the registration of cooperative societies and the detailed rules for the implementation of the Cooperative Society Law are clearly stipulated. The motive for establishing a cooperative, its objectives, the qualifications of its members, and the purity of its principles are all of great importance to the cooperative itself and its impact on society in general. It is difficult to expect progress without prior on-site investigation and careful review. In order to improve registration efficiency, the Ministry has formulated phased measures for provincial, municipal, and county bureaus to handle cooperative registration, along with a concise table, and has issued orders to the relevant provincial and municipal authorities to comply with. The Municipal Social Bureau has received this decision on registration methods, and the following is an excerpt: (A) County Government: If the number of villages with cooperatives in the county is less than one-tenth of the total number of villages in the county, or the number of cooperatives is less than thirty, it is not necessary to establish special personnel. When people apply to register a cooperative, if possible, entrust nearby cooperative promotion agencies or organizations to conduct an investigation and provide certification, and then submit it to the主管厅 for approval. If the number of villages with cooperatives in the county is more than one-tenth but less than three-tenths of the total number of villages in the county, or the number of cooperatives is less than eighty, one of the section chiefs may be designated to handle cooperative matters concurrently, or conduct the investigation themselves, or entrust nearby promotion agencies or organizations to conduct the investigation and provide certification, and then submit it to the主管厅 for approval. If the number of villages with cooperatives in the county is more than three-tenths but less than five-tenths of the total number of villages in the county, or the number of cooperatives is less than one hundred and fifty, one full-time person may be appointed, otherwise, the procedures are the same as in the previous paragraph. If the number of villages with cooperatives in the county is more than five-tenths of the total number of villages in the county, or the number of cooperatives exceeds one hundred and fifty, one to three full-time people may be appointed to directly handle the reporting. (B) 主管厅: If the number of counties with cooperatives in the province is less than one-fifth of the total number of counties in the province, it may be necessary to submit a report to the Ministry of Industry for approval. If the number of counties with cooperatives in the province is more than one-fifth but less than one-half of the total number of counties in the province, or the number of cooperatives is less than five hundred, one to two full-time people may be appointed. If the number of counties with cooperatives in the province is more than one-half but less than three-quarters of the total number of counties in the province, or the number of cooperatives is less than one thousand, two to three full-time people may be appointed. If the number of counties with cooperatives in the province is more than three-quarters of the total number of counties, or the number of cooperatives exceeds one thousand, the number of managerial personnel may be increased to five. (C) Municipal Government and Social Bureau: If the number of cooperatives established in the urban area is less than fifty, it may be handled in accordance with paragraph two of section A. The municipal government (city affiliated with the provincial government) shall consult with the主管厅 for approval, and the Social Bureau shall handle it early. If the number of cooperatives established in the urban area is more than fifty but less than one hundred, it may be handled in accordance with paragraph three of section A, otherwise, the procedures are the same as in the previous paragraph. If the number of cooperatives established in the urban area is more than one hundred, paragraph four of section A shall apply.

Foreign Sailors Commit Murder, Marine Engineering Association Petitions for Severe Punishment 124

And Requests that Cruisers be Staffed by Chinese Nationals

Foreign sailors on the Jianghai Customs Yunxing cruiser allegedly killed people under the pretext of inspecting smuggled goods in the Dinghai waters, arousing public outrage among Chinese sailors. The local sailors' party branch and the Marine Engineering Association have petitioned the central government to severely punish the foreign criminals. The Marine Engineering Association's petition is as follows: "We petition that foreign sailors on Jianghai Customs cruisers are wantonly killing innocent people and treating human life as a game. We request that they be brought to justice immediately and that all ships be staffed by Chinese nationals to prevent future incidents and uphold the sanctity of human life. We have learned that for the newly built cruisers of the Jianghai Customs, this association has previously petitioned that all crew members should be Chinese nationals. At the same time, we sent a letter to the Inspector General of Customs requesting that five ships be allocated first to be commanded by Chinese personnel. The intention of this association is none other than to recognize that foreign personnel, after all, are not of our race. Their actions are often unreasonable and deliberately contemptuous. Countless precedents in the past testify to this. Moreover, the Customs is a Chinese institution, and cruisers are Chinese ships. Their entry and exit from coastal ports are not comparable to commercial vessels, and they often involve national defense. In recent years, the skills and talents of Chinese marine engineering and navigation have emerged in large numbers, and in fact, there is no need to rely on foreign talent. The Inspector General of Customs' partiality towards foreign personnel and rejection of Chinese personnel have led to the seizure of sailors' positions and an increase in the number of unemployed people. Looking to the future, we cannot help but shudder. We believe that the ministry in charge of customs affairs should resolutely change to employing Chinese nationals for these foreign sailors who obstruct navigation, harm territorial waters, are unsuitable for the people, and waste national funds. This would not only benefit national defense but also be the hope of the entire nation. This association submitted a petition to the ministry on December 13th of last year, requesting its prompt implementation. It has been more than a month since then, and no approval has been received. Recently, we received a report that on January 13th, three foreign sailors on the Jianghai Customs Yunxing cruiser committed the crime of intentional homicide in the Zhushan Yan waters of Dinghai. The detailed facts have been published in a Shanghai newspaper on the 16th and a Ningbo newspaper on the 14th (original report attached). Thinking that the responsibility of customs cruisers is to investigate smuggling, and the natural duty of sailors is to manage the machinery, even if there is tax evasion and resistance to inspection, cruisers should aim to stop the smuggling. Even if there is resistance, bloodshed should be avoided. How can they fire bullets indiscriminately and affect the innocent? Furthermore, Liu Renyong's fishing boat had already obeyed the ship's orders, and the boatman Lou Ahe had already reached the ship's deck and was lowering the sails and dropping anchor, stopping the boat for inspection. Yet, the three Westerners still opened fire on the non-resisting people. It is clear that in their minds, they have no regard for our country or our people. Their lawlessness has reached its extreme. The result of the search was that there was no smuggling. The Westerners also knew that they had caused a major disaster. They still carried Lou Ahe, who was riddled with bullets and on the verge of death, to the Huamei Hospital in Ningbo. Disregarding the life and death of the injured person, they immediately boarded the ship and fled to Shanghai, causing Lou Ahe to die shortly after. The intentional homicide by the three Westerners is undeniable. We believe that in a republican country, the people are the main body. During the period of political tutelage, human life is the most important. Even if they were considered to be smuggling and resisting with bare hands, at most, the Westerners could only arrest the people and the boat, and our judicial organs would handle it. Moreover, Lou Ahe was a good boatman and a law-abiding citizen. Can foreign sailors freely kill people? Or is this a special right granted by the Inspector General of Customs? It is truly shocking and appalling. Those who kill should be put to death. This is a clear teaching from ancient times. Since they are employed by our country, our laws should apply to them. This association also refers to Article 26 of Chapter 2 of the new constitution announced by our country, which states, 'Any civil servant who violates the law and infringes upon the freedom or rights of the people shall be subject to criminal and civil liability in addition to disciplinary action according to law. The injured people shall also be entitled to claim compensation from the state for the damages suffered according to law.' The glorious constitution is for all people to see. Therefore, the three Westerners abused their power and killed the people, committing the crime under Article 276 of Chapter 22 of our new criminal law. We request that the ministry immediately arrest the three Westerners and send them to the court for severe punishment according to law. At the same time, all foreign sailors on the Customs cruisers should be replaced by Chinese nationals to eliminate the root of the disaster. This association is willing to be responsible for introducing marine engineering and navigation personnel with excellent skills and experience to take over the duties. This would protect the sovereignty of the coast and reduce the nation's expenditures. If we continue to condone this, or if the Inspector General of Customs intends to favor them, then the will of the nation will be a mere formality, and the lives of the people will be like weeds. We, the descendants of the gods and Chinese, will become the shooting targets of blue-eyed, yellow-bearded people. From then on, Chinese people can be slaughtered at will, and they can be trampled on everywhere. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? We believe that liberating the nation is the earnest legacy of our party's late leader. How can our people be arbitrarily killed by foreigners? We beseech your ministry to take swift action, arrest the criminals, punish them according to law, and immediately replace the foreign sailors with Chinese nationals. We will wait for your urgent orders. We respectfully submit this to the Minister of Finance Kong."

Shanghai County General Household Registration Re-check, Handling Methods for Household Changes 126

Since Shanghai County was ordered to conduct a general household registration re-check, which began on the 30th of last month, work is currently being intensified. Yesterday, the county government formulated guidelines for the general household registration re-check and ordered the districts to implement them. Among them, when re-checking household registration, the head of the household should first be asked for their name, the total number of people in the household, and the number of males and females, and these should be checked against the household registration survey form to see if they match. If the head of household has changed or the number of people in the household does not match what is stated on the household registration survey form, the following measures should be taken: If there is no change in the household and the head of household has died, a new head of household should be appointed, and the household registration survey form, joint guarantee, and house number plate should be corrected accordingly. If the entire household moves out and another new household moves in, the original survey form should be canceled and a new survey form should be filled out and a new number issued, treating the 列 number as one of the original household numbers. If the entire household moves out and no new household moves in, in addition to canceling the household registration survey form, the house number plate should be marked with the words "vacant household." If there is no change in the household but there is a change in the number of people, the original household registration survey form should be added to or canceled as appropriate: (A) If it is a birth, the date of birth should be added, and the household should be urged to correct the number of people on the house number plate at the same time. (B) If it is a death, the name of the deceased should be crossed out on the survey form and "death" should be noted in the remarks column, and the number of people on the house number plate should be corrected. (C) If someone moves in, the name, gender, age, origin, education level, occupation of the person moving in, and their relationship to the head of household should be added, and the reason for moving in and the date of moving in should be noted in the remarks column, and the number of people on the house number plate should be corrected at the same time. (D) If someone moves out, the name of the person moving out should be crossed out and "moved out" should be noted in the remarks column, and the number of days on the house number plate should be corrected. If there are more than five households with changes in each 甲, a new joint guarantee should be replaced.

Since the Shengsi Islands were placed under the jurisdiction of Zhejiang Province, the people of Jiangsu have strongly opposed it. The Shengsi Islands outside the mouth of the Yangtze River are the barrier of the Jin, Feng, Chuan, and Nan counties. During the late Qing Dynasty, they were the garrison land of Suzhou, and a general was stationed in Chongming, so the land belonged to the jurisdiction of Chong. Recently, Jiangsu Province has emphasized county and district administration, and Shengsi is the fifth district of Chongming, which is being planned. The fishing industry is relying on maintenance, but suddenly there is news that it will be placed under the rule of Zhejiang. Guojun and others dare not agree and request that the old system be maintained and no changes be made. Han Guojun, Chen Taoyi, Zhang Zhongren, Leng, Tang Wenzhi, Wang Qingmu, Lu Hao, Shi Kou.

Military and Political Department Transportation Corps Holds Coal Gas Vehicle Test 129

中华公司中華公司 (Zhonghua Company) Achieves Best Results

According to the Central News Agency, the Military and Political Department Transportation Corps has completed the coal gas vehicle test. The comparison standards are divided into three items: work efficiency, usage method, and the degree of cleanliness of the coal gas. The participants in the test were 中华煤气车公司 (Zhonghua Coal Gas Vehicle Company), 中国煤气机厂 (China Coal Gas Engine Factory), and 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop). The vehicle tested by 中华公司 (Zhonghua Company) was a General Motors truck with 76 horsepower and a load capacity of 3 tons. The vehicle tested by 中国厂 (China Factory) was a Lihe Fearless passenger car with 75 horsepower and a load capacity of 1.5 tons. The vehicle tested by 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop) was a Chevrolet truck with 70 horsepower and a load capacity of 1.5 tons. The test period was from January 13th to 21st. The test route was from Nanjing, via Shanghai and Hangzhou, and back to Nanjing, a total of 860 kilometers. The main testers were German advisor Roman, technician Shen Yunshan, Peng Hao, Hu Zongpu, and technician Wang Changcheng, among others. Detailed records were kept of the various aspects of the test. On the 13th, the vehicles gathered in Nanjing to inspect the structure of the vehicles and the coal gas stoves, and to load the vehicles with the specified amount. On the 14th, they departed from Nanjing for Shanghai. There was heavy snow that day. As a result, only one vehicle from 中华公司 (Zhonghua Company) was able to reach Shanghai. The vehicles from 中国厂 (China Factory) and 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop) experienced obstacles along the way, and switched to using gasoline to travel. They arrived in Shanghai only on the afternoon of the 15th. On the 16th, the two vehicles from 中国厂 (China Factory) and 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop) returned to their factories for repairs. The vehicle from 中华公司 (Zhonghua Company) was parked at the Xihu Company gas station at the designated location. On the morning of the 17th, they departed from Shanghai for Hangzhou. Each vehicle departed every ten minutes. The order of departure was determined by drawing lots. Also, because the Minhang ferry took time, the arrival times in Hangzhou varied. On the 18th, they drove from Hangzhou to Huzhou. That night, the vehicle from 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop) was repaired for several hours. On the 19th, they drove from Huzhou to Nanjing again. The performance of each vehicle was better, and no obstacles occurred along the way. On the 20th, the engines were disassembled in Nanjing to check the cleanliness of the coal gas. The vehicle from 中华公司 (Zhonghua Company) was the best, with no ash or dirt in the cylinder, which was no different from using gasoline. The vehicle from 中国厂 (China Factory) was second, and the vehicle from 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop) was the worst. On the 21st, the vehicles would be driven to Tangshan again for a final test ride by senior officials. The vehicle from 仲明工场 (Zhongming Workshop) did not participate due to an accident. The calculation method for work efficiency was to divide the weight carried by the distance traveled by the time spent and the horsepower of the vehicle. The vehicle from 中华公司 (Zhonghua Company) carried twice the weight of the other two vehicles, and the total time spent driving was also shorter because no obstacles occurred along the way. As a result, the vehicle from 中华公司 (Zhonghua Company) was better than the other two. All parties were satisfied and believed that the charcoal vehicle, after this heavy-duty long-distance test, could prove to be practical and beneficial to both national defense and the economy. It was decided to adopt it in large quantities.

Municipal Finance Bureau to Collect Spring House Tax Starting Today 135

2% Fine Will Be Added After More Than 10 Days

In order to collect the spring house tax, the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau issued Notice No. 238 yesterday, stating that the Municipal House Tax Improvement Collection Method has been announced by the Bureau. It is now decided to start collecting the house tax for this year's spring season on February 3. For those with a tax amount of more than 10 yuan, the Bureau's various inspection offices will fill out and issue a notice book at the time of collection, limiting the taxpayers to pay at the office within 15 days. If the limit is exceeded by more than 10 days, personnel will be dispatched to the door to collect the tax, and a fine of 2% of the tax amount will be added to warn against procrastination. For those with a tax amount of less than 10 yuan, personnel will still be dispatched to collect the tax. Those who pay at the office themselves will be allowed. In addition to the inspection offices filling out the notice forms with the amount of house tax to be paid by each household and delivering them to each household, and the Bureau issuing a notice, the date of commencement of collection and the addresses of the Bureau's various inspection offices are hereby notified: Municipal East Inspection Office, No. 43, Pudong Chunjiang Wharf; Municipal South Inspection Office, No. 29, Hunan Maojia Alley; Municipal West Inspection Office, No. 501, Robison Road, West Shanghai; Municipal North Inspection Office, No. 110, Datong Road, Zhabei.

After the Huang Automobile Company Closed Down, the Court Ruled Bankruptcy 137

At the Request of Creditor Texaco

Creditors' Meeting Scheduled for the 29th of this Month

Since the China Public Huang Automobile Company closed down, the creditor Texaco Shantou Company filed an application with the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special Zone District Court to declare the Huang Automobile Company bankrupt. The court accepted it. According to a reporter from Datong News Agency, the Second Special Court has approved the creditor's application and ruled the Huang Automobile Company bankrupt, and has scheduled the first creditors' meeting for the 29th of this month to carry out the bankruptcy procedure. The ruling text is as follows: Ruling Text: The China Public Huang Automobile Company should be declared bankrupt. Xie Lin, accountant, is appointed as the bankruptcy administrator. The address and office of the bankruptcy administrator are located at No. 723, Continental Commercial Plaza. The period for reporting claims is from December 30, 1935, to February 25, 1936. The date of the first creditors' meeting is 3:00 pm on February 29, 1936 (in the Fourth Civil Chamber of this Court). The debtors of the China Public Huang Automobile Company and the holders of property belonging to the bankrupt estate shall not make payments to the China Public Huang Automobile Company or deliver its property, and shall immediately return it or notify the bankruptcy administrator. The creditors of the China Public Huang Automobile Company shall report their claims to the bankruptcy administrator within the prescribed period. Those who fail to report within the prescribed period shall not be entitled to compensation from the bankrupt estate. Judge Wang Simo.

Wu Family Lane: Gambling Bust Uncovers Gunfire 138

A Gambler Wounded in the Left Leg by a Bullet

The Proprietor and Shooter Both Fled

In Wu Family Lane, located at the intersection of the Shanghai Municipal and Minhang County border on the Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe long-distance bus route, Zhao Bingnian, a former Public Security Bureau police officer who had been dismissed, was operating a teahouse. Adjacent to it was the temporary office of the Caojing District Defense Corps, but no corps members were stationed there. Zhao took advantage of this opportunity during the recent Lunar New Year to gather people for gambling and skimming profits. This was discovered by the Caojing District Police Station, which dispatched officers around 10 PM last night to apprehend the gamblers. The gamblers, upon suddenly seeing the police, scrambled to escape, causing great disorder. Amidst the chaos, a gunshot suddenly rang out, and a bullet struck Wu Adi (also known as A Xiaonian, 28 years old, residing in Wu Family Lane), wounding his left leg and causing him to fall to the ground. Upon hearing the gunshot, the police immediately prepared for action and began searching for the shooter, but he had already taken the opportunity to flee. The proprietor, Zhao Bingnian, also escaped during the confusion. The police took six individuals, including a Mr. Li, who were present at the gambling den, along with the gambling paraphernalia, to the station for interrogation. The wounded Wu Adi was transported overnight by car to a Shanghai hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injury was to the leg, and the bullet was extracted yesterday. After applying medication and bandaging, he was discharged and returned home. Currently, the police station is conducting a rigorous investigation to apprehend the shooter and Zhao Bingnian, the operator of the teahouse, to bring them to justice.

Customs General Tax Department Proclamation: New Buoys Installed in Tongzhou Waterway 139

Implementation Scheduled Around the 13th

The Customs General Tax Department announces that, following a re-survey of the Tongzhou waterway in the Yangtze River, buoys are being installed in the West Channel, and existing buoys will be moved. This is scheduled to be implemented around the 13th of this month. The proclamation from the Department's Maritime Affairs Section is excerpted below: It has been found, after a re-survey of the Tongzhou waterway of the Yangtze River under the jurisdiction of the Jianghai Customs and Zhenjiang Customs, that there is a West Channel upstream of the Xianfu shoal. Buoys should be installed in this West Channel, and existing buoys in the vicinity should also be moved to facilitate navigation. All matters concerning the installation, relocation, and dates are listed below for the information of all merchants. This is a special proclamation. Details are as follows: (A) Buoys to be moved: Turning Buoy: From its new location, it bears 357 degrees true north from the Langshan Pagoda, at a distance of 4.45 nautical miles, to indicate the right side of the East Channel for upstream vessels. Its color will change from black to red, with all other aspects remaining the same. Xian Buoy: From its new location, it bears half a degree true north from the Langshan Pagoda, at a distance of 6.35 nautical miles, to indicate the left side of the East Channel for upstream vessels and the left side of the entrance to the West Channel. All other aspects remain the same. (B) Buoys to be installed: West Channel Buoy: This is a lighted buoy, painted red, emitting a white flash every eight seconds, with each flash lasting four seconds. From its location, it bears 12.5 degrees true north from the Langshan Pagoda, at a distance of 5.8 nautical miles. Center Buoy: This is a lighted buoy, painted black, emitting a white flash once every eight seconds, with each flash lasting four seconds. From its location, it bears 30.5 degrees true north from the Langshan Pagoda, at a distance of 5.7 nautical miles. Guidance Buoy: This is a lighted buoy, painted red, emitting a white flash once every eight seconds, with each flash lasting four seconds. From its location, it bears 74.5 degrees true north from the Langshan Pagoda, at a distance of 3.9 nautical miles. (C) Implementation Date: Around February 13th of this year. No further announcement will be made at that time. (D) Relevant Charts: Hydrographic Charts Nos. 142 and 143 of the Ministry of Navy of the Republic of China. Canal, Maritime Affairs Section, Patrol Engineer.

Zhuanqiao Marriage Reform Association: Revised Covenant and Rituals 140

Clothing Materials Must Use Domestic Goods

The Zhuanqiao Marriage Reform Association of Shanghai County has been diligently reforming marriage customs since its establishment, earning the praise of the local populace. To further its work, the Association has specifically revised the covenant and rituals, and has reported them to the County Party Headquarters, County Government, and County Education Bureau for record and implementation. The covenant and rituals are excerpted below:

Covenant: The minimum age for marriage is 20 for men and 18 for women. Marriage ceremonies must follow the regulations stipulated by this Association. At the wedding, Association badges must be worn. The wedding ceremony is limited to one hour. Wedding attire must conform to national dress codes, and materials must be domestic goods. If the bride's family provides a dowry, it must be practical and limited to domestic goods. Banquet meals must not exceed four yuan per table. Gifts between members are limited to one yuan (exceptions for special relationships). If a member requires assistance from the Association for their wedding, they must notify the Association one week in advance. All members of the Association must be literate. Those who are illiterate must learn to read after joining the Association. Association staff assisting with members' weddings need not give gifts. Members are not allowed to hire musicians, incense table attendants, or firecrackers for weddings. If they must use them, they must pay two yuan to the Association's fund. If only an incense table is used and no musicians are hired, the fee is waived. Members are not allowed to imitate dual morning ceremonies for weddings. Violators must pay five yuan to the Association's fund. The "teasing the bride" custom is limited to midnight on the wedding day and must not extend beyond that time.

Rituals: (1) Performing the wedding ceremony; (2) Playing stringed instruments or music; (3) Ushers taking their seats; (4) Guests taking their seats; (5) The master of ceremonies taking their seat; (6) The introducer taking their seat; (7) The representative of the Marriage Reform Association taking their seat; (8) The officiant taking their seat; (9) The male and female guides leading the bride and groom to their seats; (10) Playing stringed instruments or music; (11) All attendees facing inward, standing at attention towards the portrait of Sun Yat-sen and the national flag, and performing the salutation ceremony with three bows; (12) All return to their places; (13) The introducer delivers a speech; (14) The groom turns right, the bride turns left, facing each other and performing the wedding ceremony with three bows; (15) The bride and groom return to their places and sit down; (16) The officiant reads the certificate; (17) The groom affixes his seal; (18) The bride affixes her seal; (19) The officiant affixes his seal; (20) The introducer affixes his seal; (21) The master of ceremonies affixes his seal; (22) Playing music; (23) The officiant exchanges souvenirs for the bride and groom; (24) The officiant delivers a speech; (26) The representative of the Marriage Reform Association delivers a speech; (27) Guests give speeches; (28) The bride and groom deliver thank-you speeches; (29) Playing music; (30) The officiant presents the certificate to the master of ceremonies; (31) The bride and groom thank the officiant with a bow; (32) The officiant exits; (33) The introducer exits; (34) The bride and groom thank the representative of the Marriage Reform Association with a bow; (35) The representative of the Marriage Reform Association exits; (36) The bride and groom thank the master of ceremonies with a bow; (37) Playing music.

An examination will be scheduled to determine acceptance.

Recent Financial Situation of Shanghai County

Since the municipal boundary demarcation, the major tax sources of Shanghai County have been incorporated into the municipal area. Although the municipality provides an annual subsidy of 50,000 yuan in accordance with the agreement, this is ten times less than the previous situation. The recent situation of Shanghai County is reported below: Income: Provincial tax revenue: 153,400 yuan; Local revenue: 279,123 yuan. Major taxes: Land tax: 247,123 yuan; Deed tax: 27,000 yuan; Slaughter tax: 8,100 yuan; Miscellaneous taxes: 7,100 yuan; Local tax: 53,000 yuan; Subsidies: 54,000 yuan; Temporary income: 36,200 yuan. Case of a Young Woman Stabbed to Death: Discovery of the Murderer's Suicide Note 142

The Note Stated the Deceased Was a 17-Year-Old Cigarette Factory Worker

Jealousy Over Her Relationship With Another Man Led the Murderer to Lure Her to a Hotel and Kill Her

In room 54 (reported as 45 in yesterday's news) of the Anshang Hotel on Balizhao Street in the French Concession, a female guest was fatally stabbed by a man who had accompanied her. The murderer fled. The incident was discovered by a waiter, Chen Jinyu, who informed the accountant, who reported it to the French police. Chinese and foreign detectives rushed to the scene to investigate, and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Mortuary for examination. It was reported yesterday that the case would be reported to the Second Special District Court today for further examination and that the deceased's belongings and clothing were taken back to the police station to investigate the murderer. It is now learned that the murderer left behind a letter, which was taken back to the police station by the officers. The letter reportedly stated that the deceased's name was Zhang Fuying, 17 years old, and that she worked in a cigarette factory. The murderer had been in a romantic relationship with her since she was 14. When she was 16, she became involved with another man. The former boyfriend (the murderer now at large) then paid 5,000 yuan to have her break off the relationship with the latter. However, the deceased continued to have a secret affair with the latter, leading the murderer to resent her. He devised a plan to lure her to a hotel and kill her to vent his anger. The detailed course of events will be reported in detail three days later. When the police sent officers to the mortuary yesterday to take photos of the body, they discovered knife wounds on both palms and fingers, suggesting that the deceased was not killed while asleep but was conscious and resisted, resulting in the injuries to her hands. The French police sent Detective Bu Zhenglong to investigate in the Gaochang Temple area of Nanshi yesterday. There were no cigarette factories there except for Qichang Cigar Factory. The police then summoned Wang Maye, an employee of the cigarette factory, as well as the pimps and brothel keepers in the French Concession to the mortuary to identify the body. They all stated that they did not recognize the deceased. No one else came to identify the body.

Extortion Case of Xiang Yixin: Interrogation of the Robbers Concluded 145

Each Robber Pushes Responsibility onto Others

Investigation Reveals Involvement in Other Cases

Xiang Yixin, a Ningbo native and owner of Xingchang Iron Factory at No. 151 Oujia Road, was kidnapped in the Jiamao Temple on Gonghe Road, Zhabei, last autumn, but escaped unharmed. Thugs, however, coveted his wealth, and between October 13th and January 6th of this year, sent more than ten threatening letters demanding 80,000 yuan. After investigation by Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, Detective Liu Shaokui, Detective Qian Xianting, and Chen Yonggui of the General Inspection Office, eight suspects, including Wei Youliang, Wang Wencheng, and Xiang's son-in-law Xu Ruixiang, were arrested and detained in the Jiaxing Road and Hongkou police stations, and then transferred to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiefei presided over the trial in the Third Criminal Court. Mr. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Shanghai Municipal Council, stated that the mastermind behind the threatening letters was Xu Ruixiang. The defendant Wei Youliang wrote two letters, reducing the demand from 80,000 yuan to 20,000 yuan. Wang Wencheng wrote three letters, initially demanding 10,000 yuan, based on Xu's draft, with a promise of a 20% reward of 2,000 yuan after receipt. Wang later wrote another letter intending to obtain 5,000 yuan for himself. The last letter was written by Xu in pencil. The suspects confessed in the police station and should be severely punished according to the law. Furthermore, Gong A'gen committed a robbery on Nanjing Road on December 7th last year, stealing 60 yuan from a Mr. Cao at No. 541. The letters were presented for inspection. Xiang Yixin stated that Xu Ruixiang was indeed his son-in-law, but his daughter passed away nine years ago, leaving a granddaughter. Xu had borrowed a total of more than 4,000 yuan from him. After his kidnapping last autumn, he asked Xu to work in the factory with a monthly salary of 16 yuan. After receiving the threatening letters, Xu was the one who went to negotiate several times. Wei Youliang confessed that Wang Jinzhang brought the drafts of the threatening letters and that he wrote two of them. Wang Jinzhang and Zhang Guan'gen claimed that Gong A'gen was the source of the drafts, and they did not know anything else. Gong A'gen confessed that Xue Shandong, who is at large, brought the drafts, mentioning that Xiang's son-in-law Xu was an informant. He only received six yuan after the Nanjing Road robbery. Wang Wencheng confessed that Xu wrote the drafts of the threatening letters and asked him to copy them. Liu Shanshu and Yang Fuchen testified that they knew Xu had asked Wang Wencheng to write the threatening letters at Wang's residence, but they did not participate. Lawyer Yan Fangang defended Xu Ruixiang, whose testimony was evasive and adamant in denying the charges. Judge Xiao instructed that all be remanded in custody for sentencing at a later date.

Chen Hongfu's Death by Violence Prosecuted: Prosecutor's Investigation Confirms 147

Chen Hongfu, a Chongming native residing in Yanjiacuo, Gaoqiao, Pudong, who made a living by farming, was attacked late in the evening of November 27th of last year, resulting in two broken ribs and immediate death. His body was abandoned on the roadside, making it a suspicious case. The next day, the local security chief reported the incident to the local court, which dispatched Prosecutor Li Fen to the scene for examination. The prosecutor noted that the deceased's wife, Chen Huangshi, did not seek justice for her husband's wrongful death and seemed indifferent and without grief, which raised suspicion. After the local police station summoned her for questioning, she claimed that her husband had been caught stealing taro from someone else's field and was beaten to death. To ascertain the truth, the police sent officers to her home to investigate and found half a sack of taro. After a thorough investigation, it became clear that her statement was false and that the taro belonged to the deceased. Suspicion of other circumstances arose, and Chen Huangshi was detained and sent to court for questioning. Since the tragic incident, there has been much speculation in the area, with some claiming that the deceased was secretly murdered by his wife, Chen Huangshi, and her maternal uncle, Lu Zhiliang, and others due to a rent debt Chen owed Lu. Lu Zhiliang was subsequently arrested and detained for questioning. The judge, considering the seriousness of the case, instructed the warden of the detention center to suspend visits for both Lu Zhiliang and Chen Huangshi to prevent collusion. Meanwhile, key witnesses, such as Zhang Qinglang and Yang the Blind, were summoned and questioned repeatedly. It has now been learned that Prosecutor Li Fen has spared no effort to investigate the case in detail, personally conducting on-site investigations and repeatedly summoning the deceased's children and witnesses to the court for detailed questioning. He filed a public prosecution on the preceding day and the public trial should take place soon.

National Association of Western Medicine Representatives Go to Beijing to Petition 148

Presenting Three Major Reasons to Advocate for Physicians Nationwide

Yesterday, the Chinese Western Medicine Association, in accordance with the resolutions of the Third National Representative Congress, appealed to all senior central government agencies to grant medical licenses to all practicing physicians so that they can serve society with peace of mind. In addition to representatives from provinces, cities, and counties gathering at the Central Hotel in Beijing, the association's representatives, including Qian Longzhang, Nong Shisong, Liu Renfu, Zhu Bin, Hong Xichun, Zhang Guowei, Liu Xinbai, Wu Jingcun, and Secretary Qiu Pingsan, traveled to Beijing by overnight train last night with a petition and letters to important figures. The original text is as follows: The petition states that, given the vast territory of our country and the negligence of inland administration, the number of Western-trained physicians is insufficient to meet the needs of the entire country. Therefore, we request that those who have been practicing Western medicine for the past eighteen years be granted licenses to practice medicine, and that those who have been practicing medicine since then be provided with relief and that flexible measures be re-issued to meet the needs of society. It has been noted that, since the promulgation of the Provisional Regulations for Physicians by the Ministry of Health in 1929, it has been difficult to implement due to its incompatibility with the immature state of medicine in our country. Subsequently, in 1932, the Executive Yuan passed two directives on flexible licensing of physicians, issued by the Ministry of Interior. These directives stated that "Our country has a vast territory and too few qualified physicians. Many have graduated from unapproved medical schools or have come from hospitals, and many of them have rich experience and are valuable talents. If we do not find a way out for them and order them to stop practicing, those with actual medical abilities will inevitably suffer injustice. At a time when there is a shortage of physicians, how can we meet the needs of society? It is the duty of the Ministry to consider the needs of the people and seek practical solutions, so we have formulated two flexible licensing methods" (omitted). At the time, administrative offices in various places, except for major trading ports, mostly treated the directives as mere formalities, not essential, and shelved them, failing to report or publicize them, causing Western-trained physicians in the interior who met the flexible qualifications to miss the statutory opportunity. This was even more true in remote provinces and counties where the atmosphere was closed. Now, county governments are using the regulations to crack down and force physicians to stop practicing. The original intent of a country's government and its decrees is to promote benefits and eliminate harms. Since the promulgation of the Provisional Regulations for Physicians, benefits have not been seen, but harms have proliferated. To adopt the decrees of other countries that have undergone repeated reforms and implement them in our country with immature medicine is like forcing people to cut their feet to fit their shoes. Before the shoes fit, the feet are already injured. Everyone knows this is impossible. Moreover, each country has its own national conditions. Looking back to the past and examining the abuses, this is the first reason why we should request the re-issuance of secondary flexible licensing methods for physicians to eliminate abuses. Moreover, the current number of Western-trained physicians in our country is truly insufficient to meet the needs of the entire country. Whenever epidemics and diseases break out in the interior, the public relies entirely on this small number of Western-trained physicians to administer injections and provide emergency care. They are truly as rare as phoenix feathers and as compassionate as Buddha. Furthermore, the central national defense design agencies are actively designing and concentrating technical talents to respond to the changing circumstances. If the local county governments are allowed to force them to stop practicing, it would cause those with real talents and experience to be buried and suffer injustice. It does not conform to the national policy of caring for the needs of the people and seeking practical solutions. This is the second reason why we should request the re-issuance of flexible methods and provide relief to already practicing physicians, supplement registration, protect national talent, and meet the needs of the people. It has been reported that the State Council has promulgated the Regulations for Traditional Chinese Medicine, which state that "Article 1: Before the Examination Yuan holds examinations for traditional Chinese medicine, anyone who is at least 25 years old and has one of the following qualifications may practice traditional Chinese medicine after being examined and certified by the Ministry of Interior: Those who have passed the examination or assessment for traditional Chinese medicine by the central or provincial governments and have a certificate; Those who have been issued a license to practice medicine by the central or provincial governments; Those who have graduated from a traditional Chinese medicine school and have a certificate; Those who have been practicing traditional Chinese medicine for more than five years." All have the possibility of being granted a license. Compared to the Regulations for Western Medicine: Those who have graduated from a national or government-approved public or private medical school for more than five years and have a diploma; Those who have graduated from a government-approved private medical school in a foreign country for more than five years and have a diploma, or those who have a physician's license from a foreign government; Foreigners who have a physician's license from their respective governments and have a certificate from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Those who have passed the physician's examination and have a certificate, there is a vast difference. Western-trained physicians, who are also citizens and serve under the banner of Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People, are treated so differently. What could be more unfair? Moreover, in the late Qing Dynasty, our country had no medical school facilities, let alone approved or unapproved ones. Even in the recent reform of the political system, the number of medical schools run by the state is few and far between. Furthermore, the regulations were promulgated eighteen years ago, and graduation requires more than five years. It is inevitable that the standards are too high. To strive to align our medical administration with that of European and American countries in one fell swoop is to be impatient and not to seek practical solutions. This is the third reason why we should request the re-issuance of secondary flexible licensing for physicians to maintain their profession. In this transitional era, Western-trained physicians who are needed by society should be supported and nurtured, treated equally, and the innocent should be protected. Those who have been practicing medicine for more than 18 years should all be granted licenses, and those who have been practicing medicine since then should also be provided with relief. To save the people is to save the country (and those who have been practicing medicine for the past eighteen years have six years of experience, which is more than the five-year limit for granting licenses to traditional Chinese medicine practitioners. It cannot be said to be excessive in terms of both reason and sentiment). This association, in accordance with the suggestions and resolutions passed by the delegates from all provinces, cities, and counties at the Third National Western Medicine Representative Congress on New Year's Day, and the petition filed by the representatives, respectfully petitions the government to consider the needs of the people, graciously approve the issuance of medical licenses, so that everyone can serve society with peace of mind, so that it will be fair, practical, and beneficial to the public and private sectors. Respectfully presented to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Health. The Executive Committee of the Chinese Western Medicine Association and the delegates of the Third National Congress respectfully kowtow. Chairman Qian Longzhang, February 2, 1936.

Flourishing Exhibition of Japanese-Influenced Chinese Medicine: Second Day Success 149

The New Drug Association Requests That the Enforcement of Registered Patent Medicines Be Delayed Until the Deadline 150

The National New Drug Industry Association submitted a report to the Ministry of Health yesterday, stating that the deadline for patent medicine registration by its member associations was the end of last year. However, the number of patent medicine types is extremely large, and very few members have received licenses. The main reason for this is that the procedures for revising prescriptions and amending instructions are quite complicated and cannot be completed in time. Therefore, on November 27 last year, the association submitted a report to your ministry, expressing its difficulties and requesting that the deadline be extended. Your ministry graciously considered the situation and issued Medical Document No. 2185 on December 7 last year, extending the deadline by six months and reporting to the Executive Yuan for record. In accordance with this, the association has forwarded the approved documents to inform drug merchants in various places. However, drug merchants in various places have recently reported that military and police authorities in various places, not understanding the people's livelihood, are still rashly enforcing bans based on the Regulations for the Management of Patent Medicines during this extended registration period, which is having a significant impact on business. Therefore, they request that the association submit another report to your ministry, asking you to consider the situation and promptly issue a notice to the governments of all provinces, cities, and counties, instructing them not to enforce bans rashly before the deadline for patent medicine registration, in order to maintain business.

Liu Zhongying, Executive Committee Member of the Ratepayers' Association, Suggests Changing Rickshaw Pullers' Armbands to Numbered Uniforms 151

More Attractive and More Practical

The Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession started registering rickshaw pullers last year. Registered rickshaw pullers must pay a fee of one yuan, and the Municipal Council will give the rickshaw puller a magnetic armband for identification. Anyone who has not registered and obtained this armband is not allowed to work. Now, Mr. Liu Zhongying, an executive committee member of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association in the Concession, believes that armbands are easily lost. He specially suggested that the Ratepayers' Association ask the Municipal Council to change this registration fee to make rickshaw pullers' numbered uniforms, which would be distributed to each rickshaw puller to wear while working, in order to show consideration for laborers and further enhance the appearance of the city. The original letter from Mr. Liu to the Ratepayers' Association is recorded below: "Sir, I would like to inform you that the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession stipulates that, starting last year, all rickshaw pullers operating in the Concession must first register, pay a registration fee of one yuan, and obtain an armband before they can perform labor. Since the implementation, the inspection has been extremely strict, resulting in many rickshaw pullers who are unable to pay the registration fee losing their jobs. At the same time, because the registration fee is too high, rickshaw pullers in general feel overwhelmed. Moreover, the armbands that are received are easily lost due to their small size. In order to show consideration for laborers, I propose that the Municipal Council change the registration fee to make rickshaw pullers' numbered uniforms, which would be distributed to each rickshaw puller to wear while working, in place of armbands. This measure would not only enhance the appearance of the city, but also provide rickshaw pullers with practical benefits by adding a piece of clothing. Furthermore, it would not contradict the Municipal Council's policy of rectifying rickshaw affairs. Therefore, I am sending this special letter to suggest this, hoping that you will consider it."

Second Asylum for the Poor to Close in Mid-Month 157

Poor People to Be Transferred to the First Asylum

The Nanchezhan Road First Asylum for the Poor and the Xietulu Second Asylum for the Poor, which were organized by charitable organizations in this city, have been established for two months since last winter. They have accommodated poor people, with a maximum of more than 3,400 people in both asylums. The daily expenses are huge, requiring more than 20,000 yuan in funding. Now that the weather is getting warmer, some poor people have requested to leave the asylum to seek their own livelihood. There are currently only more than 2,000 people remaining in the asylum. The asylum authorities are trying to reduce expenses and plan to close the Xietulu Second Asylum for the Poor in mid-month. All poor people will be transferred to the First Asylum. Second Collection of Sixty Famous Song Dynasty Poets Published 164

Song poetry is a must-read for scholars of Chinese language, so many publishers have printed it. However, the prices are surprisingly high, and the sentences are not punctuated, which is inconvenient for beginners. Even those who study poetry must rely on poetry rules and other references. The Shanghai Magazine Company has decided to publish rare and important books of Chinese literature. It has specially invited Shi Cunshi to punctuate and carefully proofread them, and they are printed according to the Jigu Ge edition. They are divided into six collections and sold in separate volumes. The price is low, and the printing is elegant and lovely. After the first collection was published, it was reprinted in less than a month. It has also been recommended by Mu Xun, a contemporary expert in poetry, and is very popular among readers. The second collection has now been released, with individual volumes sold at 50-70 cents for the first collection and 40-55 cents for the second collection. There is a 10% discount for in-store purchases, and postage is free for out-of-town purchases. It is heard that the company is responding to the requests of more than a thousand readers in the interior and will issue a pre-order for one month. Those who pay the full pre-order price of 17 yuan can still order, and those who need postage will be charged an additional 1.5 yuan. The deadline is the end of this month.

Huiliyuan's Bestselling Aviation Lottery Tickets: The Huiliyuan Ticket Shop at the intersection of Aiduo Road and Dongxin Bridge in this city has been selling well since it sold the top two or three major prizes in the 17th issue and won the second prize in the 18th issue. The number of sales is booming every issue, and customers are crowded, and the storefront is like a market. Orders from other places are pouring in, and it is difficult to handle them all. The 19th issue is about to be drawn.

News of Painting and Calligraphy 166

Recent News of Jinshijia's Painting: Tongxin. His name is Danian, also known as Xiaosong. He is the fifth son of Sima Songjun, the former magistrate of Deqing County, and the younger brother of Shuping and Xucang, both of whom exhausted their teachers. He has a deep family background. He learned seal script at the age of eight and is proficient in the inscriptions on bronzes and stones from the Shang, Zhou, Qin, and Han dynasties. He is also good at iron calligraphy. For more than fifty years, he has been famous all over the world. In the past, he was burdened by official duties and had no time to paint. In recent years, he has been living in seclusion on the lake, and those who seek his work come one after another, leaving him no time from dawn to dusk, and he is tired of coping. Therefore, he has revised the price list and added painting. His landscapes, flowers, and fruits are all exquisite and divine, not allowing the Jinshijia of ancient and modern times to be exclusively beautiful. Those who seek his work will surely come one after another. The works can be submitted to various paper and fan shops in Shanghai and Hangzhou, as well as the Xiling Seal Society, or his residence at No. 60, Former Fan Administration, Hangzhou. Detailed price lists will be sent upon request.

Weather Report 167

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong is clear and cold, and the wind direction is uncertain, due to the low pressure passing through Mongolia and moving eastward. The weather in the Yangtze River basin is clear and cold, sometimes turning cloudy, with fog in the morning, and the wind is slight and unstable. Here, there are northwest to northeast winds. The weather in the East China Sea and Taiwan is cloudy, with strong winter monsoons. Also, within the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was a maximum of 43.2 and a minimum of 23.9. On the same day last year, the maximum was 44.1 and the minimum was 38.3.

Letter 168

We found that in the Shanghai news section of your newspaper on the 28th of last month, there was a news item about postal service workers Zhou Changfa, Gao Fanqing, and Hu Jintang colluding to open customers' letters and misappropriate stamps. Zhou Changfa is a temporary employee of our bureau, while Gao Fanqing and Hu Jintang are actually Gao Huaiqing and Wu Jintang by mistake. They are postal service workers of our bureau, not mail carriers. We are sending this letter to request that you check and correct this immediately in order to conform to the facts. This is addressed to the editorial department of the Shenbao Newspaper. Shanghai Postal Administration. February 1, 25th year of the Republic of China. No. 714.

Zhejiang University President Guo Renyuan Resumes Duty; Turmoil Completely Subsided; Classes Scheduled to Resume on the 11th 171

The turmoil at Zhejiang University has lasted for a month. When President Jiang visited Hangzhou in the latter part of last month, he went to the university and convened a student meeting to lecture them. After that, the turmoil completely subsided. The student self-government association took the lead in expelling two students in accordance with the Ministry of Education's order. Subsequently, after mediation by the authorities, the two students submitted letters of repentance to the president and faculty members, and they were temporarily allowed to resume their studies. President Guo Renyuan has arrived at the university to resume his duties and has appointed Cai Bao as the Dean of the College of Liberal Arts and Zheng Zonghai as the Dean of Academic Affairs. Classes began on February 1st, and the semester exams for the first semester were held on February 3rd and completed on the 9th. Formal classes will resume on the 11th. As for the previously organized school affairs meeting, it will be dissolved after the organization of the academic affairs meeting is established.
